1b1(phal chen): 'phags pa sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba/ bam pa
1b2(phal chen): drug cu rtsa gsum pa// / de nas byang chub sems dpa'i tshigs
1b3(phal chen): po de'i nang nas// byang chub sems dpa'i kha cig 'di snyam du sems te//
2a1(phal chen): #/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing ni rnga
2a2(phal chen): tsam zhig tu bsam gyi sa mi khyab/ sangs rgas brtse ma ldan 'das rnams kyi sngon gyi smon
2a3(phal chen): lam dang / 'byung ba rnam par dag pa ni dzi tsa zhog tu bas mgyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas
2a4(phal chen): bcom ldan 'dis rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i gdung ni ji tsa mo zhig tu bas so
2b1(phal chen): gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas skye ba ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis
2b2(phal chen): mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshogaso pa'i sku ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis
2b3(phal chen): mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam
2b4(phal chen): gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes ni ji tsam zhig tu
2b5(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa
3a1(phal chen): ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa mi mnga' ba'i rnam
3a2(phal chen): par spyod pa ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa ni ji tsam zhig
3a3(phal chen): tu bsam gyis mi khyab snyam pa dang / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' de dag gi sems thugs kyis
3a4(phal chen): thugs su chud nas/ byang chub sems dpa' ut+pa la'i snying po sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis byin du brlabs so// sangs
3a5(phal chen): rgyas kyi ye shes kyi byin dang ldan par mdzad do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od kyis snang bar mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi gzi brjid kyis
3a6(phal chen): yongs su rgyas par mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi mi 'jigs pa la rab tu bzhag go// sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa
3b1(phal chen): khong du chud par mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba nyid dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi yul rab tu rtogs par mdzad do// chags pa med pa'i rgyud 'byam klas pa la rab tu bzhag go// sangs rgyas
3b2(phal chen): thams cad gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa'i rigs rab tu rtogs par mdzad de// sangs rgyas kyi tshul gyi gnas brjod du med pa la rab tu bzhag pa mdzad do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' ud+d+ha
3b3(phal chen): la'i snying pos chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa rig cing khong du chud pas/ chags pa med pa'i dbyings su bsgrubs pa'i yid dang / chos thams cad la bsgribs pa med par gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
3b4(phal chen): spyod pa dang / kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang ldan pa'i yang dgu par 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas tham cad kyi rjes su song ba'i sangs rgyas blta ba dang / snying rje chen pos lta ba'i sems can thams cad
3b5(phal chen): yongs su sbyong ba'i go cha chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yi dam dang / spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor rgyun chad pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa skad cig gi cha shas la rnam par
3b6(phal chen): spyod pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sgo mthong ba mi zad pa dang / tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa'i rnam pa gzungs thams cad kyis snang bar byas pa dang ldan pas/ sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub sems
3b7(phal chen): dpa' pad+mo'i snying po la 'di skad ces smras so// kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni tshad med pa la rnam par spyod pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
4a1(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa chen po la rnam par spyod pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa thams cad la sku'i
4a2(phal chen): mtshan nyid thams cad rab tu brnyes pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba ni ti nge 'dzin dang dgongs pas sbyar ba'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
4a3(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa bzhi ni brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa shin tu ston pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la
4a4(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab par rnam par spyod pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi gsung dang dbyangs ni tshad med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
4a5(phal chen): kyis chos kyi dbyings thugs su chud ba ni brjod du med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba ni thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa'o//
4a6(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis chos kyi dbyings thugs su chud cing bstan pa ni sgribs pa meng po'i mthar thug pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di
4a7(phal chen): bdag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnam pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam
4b1(phal chen): kyi gzugs kyi sku rnam par dag pa ni/ rnyog pa med par rgyud thams cad du byung bas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa med pa'i spyan ni
4b2(phal chen): chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi spyan mngon par sangs rgyas pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa med pa'i snyan ni/ 'gro ba thams
4b3(phal chen): cad kyi sgra sgribs pa med par thugs su chud pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shangs kyi skye mched ni/ sangs rgyas kyi mnga' thams cad
4b4(phal chen): kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ljags shin tu yangs pa ni/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du gsung gi dbyangs
4b5(phal chen): rjes su 'gro bas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i chos nyid ni/ sems can thams cad ma lus pa'i sems kyi rnam pa de bzhin gshegs pa mthong
4b6(phal chen): ba rnam par dmigs pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi 'phrin las ni/ chos kyi sku dang tha mi dad cing dus gsum chags pa med par
4b7(phal chen): thugs su chud cing rnam par dag pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa bsgrings pa mi mnga' ba la rnam par spyod pa ni/
5a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang dang / rnam par 'phrul pa dang / cho 'phrul mi zad pa yang dag par ston pas mthura' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
5a2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rnam par dag pa ni/ brjod du med pa'i rgyan byin gyis brlabs pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa yang dag par bstan te/
5a3(phal chen): bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par dmigs par mdzad pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i khyad par dang / smon lam thams cad
5a4(phal chen): yongs su rdzogs pa ni/ rnam par rol pa'i ye shes kyi chos yongs su rdzogs te/ chos thams cad rdzogs par byang chub par bya ba la mtha' dang dbus med pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/
5a5(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di ngas
5a6(phal chen): ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi skang cig sa ye shes kyis mngon par bsgrungs pa yang ngas par bldan pa'o// brgya ba zhen/ gang cig gcig la 'di brten gyi khams rnams cad /
5a7(phal chen): drung ba ldar kyo banas nas 'phob yongs su bstan pa dang / gang cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi mas thams cad du byang chubasams dpa'i tsha yongs su bstan pa dang / gang cis bcog pa 'jis ce gying/
5b1(phal chen): thams cad du mngon par 'byung ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byang chub kyi shing drung du bzhugs shing mngon par 'tshang rgya ba yongs su bstan pa dang / sa/
5b2(phal chen): cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'dul ba'i sems can yongs su smin pa'i tshu /
5b3(phal chen): lta ba bzhin du dus la bab par shes pas/ sangs rgyas bsnyen bkur ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du sems can ji ltar 'dul ba'i tshul bzhin du de bzhin
5b4(phal chen): gshegs pa brjod du med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi sku sna tshogs rnam par dmigs pa yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rgyan sna tshogs dang / rgyan brjod du
5b5(phal chen): med pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i mdzod yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rnam par dag pa gcig ma
5b6(phal chen): yin pa thams cad yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad du dbang po dang brtso
5b7(phal chen): 'grus rnam pa tha dang byung ba dang / mos pa dang spyod pa rnam pa tha dad pa byung ba la dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyung du mngon par 'tshang rgyab yongs su bstan pa ste/ kyo rgyal ba'i sras bcu po dag ni
6a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi skad cig la ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa yang dag par bstan pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po
6a2(phal chen): 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'da' ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mngon par 'tshang rgya ba ni de'i dus las mi 'da'
6a3(phal chen): bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dge ba rnam par smin pa dang / rnam par smin pa mnyam pa nyid ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs
6a4(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yongs su smin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams lung bstan pa ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
6a5(phal chen): rnams kyis sems can gyi bsam pa'i rgyud du cho 'phrul yongs su bstan pa ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can mos pa ji lta/
6a6(phal chen): bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sku yongs su bstan pa ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams btang snyoms su bzhugs pa ni de'i dus las mi
6a7(phal chen): 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams yul dang / grong dang / grong rdal du gshegs pa ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas
6b1(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams dad pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can yongs su 'dzin pa ni de'i dus las mi 'anga' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems
6b2(phal chen): can kun nas nyon mongs pa dang ldan zhing gdul dka' ba la gzhan la ltos pa mi mnga' bar 'dul ba ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
6b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas rnam par 'phrul pa bstan pa ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs
6b4(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'da' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dang
6b5(phal chen): med cing bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par skyil mo krung gcig gis rgyas par dgang ba dang / dus gcig tu sangs rgyas thams cad yongs su bstan pa
6b6(phal chen): dang / 'od zer gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa tham cad snang bar bya ba dang / sku gzugs gcig gis lus dang gzugs thams cad yongs su bstan pa dang / gnas gcig na bzhugs kyang 'jig
6b7(phal chen): rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par byon pa'i skur 'gyur ba dang / ye shes gcig rtogs pos chos thams cad la bsgribs pa med par 'gyur ba dang / thugs gcig bskyed pas chos kyi dbyings thams cad /
7a1(phal chen): ma lus par rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi che ba nyid tshad med pa dang ldan pa'i gshegs stabs gcig gis de khon nyid yang dag par bstan pa dang
7a2(phal chen): dus gsum thams cad sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang gis rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad dang ma 'dres par bzhugs shing / 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i
7a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis rgyud kyi tshul gcig pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dpe
7a4(phal chen): med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes te/
7a5(phal chen): bcu gang zhe na/ 'jug pa med pa'i chos thams cad la 'jug pas smon lam mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / lus med pa la lus mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad mig rdzi
7a6(phal chen): pa la mngon par 'tshang rgya ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / sems can gyi mthar thug par bdag med pa la sems can 'dul ba mngon par bsgrub po'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad mtshan ma
7a7(phal chen): med pa la mtshan ma sna tshogs mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / 'jig rten gyi 'ams kyi yul ma skyes pa la 'jig rten gyi khams 'du ba dang 'jig pa mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / yul ba
7b1(phal chen): cang mngon par 'du bya ba med pa la las kyi rnam par smin pa mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad brjod du med pa la chos kyi dbyings su gsung mngon par sdu pa'i ye shes dang / chos tham
7b2(phal chen): cad kun nas nyon mongs pa dang rnam par byang bas 'jug pa med pa la kun nas nyod mongs pa dang rnam par byang ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad ma skyes pa la skye ba dang 'jig pa'i mtshan nyid
7b3(phal chen): rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes so//
7b4(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshad med pa khongs su chud pa dag ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku ni dus gsum thams cad kyi
7b5(phal chen): rjes su 'brang ba'i khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can thams cad 'dul bar mdzad pa ni cho 'phrul chen po gsum gyi khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
7b6(phal chen): rnams tshig rab tu dbye ba thams cad la mkhas pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi gzungs thams cad kyi khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo thams cad ni de bzhin
7b7(phal chen): gshegs pa'i tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa bzhir khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can thams cad yongs su mi gtong ba ni thugs rje chen po'i khongs su chud pa yin/
8a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams cag tu mnyam par gzhag pa ni dus thams cung du sems can thams cad la rnam par gzigs pa'i yongs su chung ba yin/ sangs rgyas /
8a2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dge ba'i rtsa bar ni sems can rnam par 'dul ba thams cad ljongs su chung ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa mi mnga' bar stong pa ni chos kyi dbyings
8a3(phal chen): thams cad khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi skad cig gcig tu ni 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad khongs su chud pa yin
8a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi nyi ma gcig tu ni dus gsum gyi bskal pa'i grangs khongs su chud par bstan pa thams cad 'ongs su chud pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
8a5(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi tshad med pa'i khongs su chud pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di ga ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba rnams te/ @
8a6(phal chen): gang zhe na/ bdud kyi dkrugs ma rab tu 'joms shing rnam par 'thor ba ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// mu stegs can gzhan dang phas kyi rgol ba tsha
8a7(phal chen): cad pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// 'dul ba'i sems can thams cad rab tu tshim par mdzad pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin
8b1(phal chen): tu che ba'i chos brjod pa dadaka' ba'o// sems can 'dul ba'i dbang gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du bgashegs pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu che ba'i chos bzod /
8b2(phal chen): par dka' ba'o// chos kyi dbyings thubs su chud pa'i ye shes ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par
8b3(phal chen): skus khyab cing / sangs rgyas kyi sku rnam par phye ba sna tshogs thams cad du mi gnyis pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgyu che ba'i chos bathod pa dga' ba'o// gsung gi yan lag rnams
8b4(phal chen): cad la sems can mos par bya ba dang / thos par bya ba dang / gdul bar bya ba don yod par tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa thogs pa med pas bstan pa'i tshul du tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa bzhi 'byung
8b5(phal chen): ba ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ba spu'i bu ga gcig nas de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams
8b6(phal chen): thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bsam gyis mi khyab cing / thogs pa med pa'i tshul du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba skyed kyi thabs kyis 'byung zhing / de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi
8b7(phal chen): sku'i ba spu'i bu ga thams cad nas 'byung ba ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
9a1(phal chen): pa'i sangs rgyas rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra bskyed yongs su ston cing / sangs rgyas kyi
9a2(phal chen): rgyan dang / rang bzhin gyi lngab lbub dang / chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba rgyun mi 'chad cing sem can rnam par 'dul ba thogs pa med la/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag tu gtogs pa rnams la
9a3(phal chen): la'ang mi bde ba dang gnod pa med kyang rdul shin tu phra ba de'ang yangs par mi byas/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag kyang chung bar ma byas par ji ltar gnas pa'i chos kyi dbyings kyang thugs su chud ba'i
9a4(phal chen): ye shes mnga' ba ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// mun pa med pa'i khams de bzhin gshegs pas mngon par sangs rgyas te/ sangs/
9a5(phal chen): rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mun pa med cing bsgribs pa mi mnga' la/ sems can pha rol gyi bsgribs pa sna tshogs kyi gnas par sel na/ de la bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs
9a6(phal chen): bcu dang ldan pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos la bzod par dka' ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu
9a7(phal chen): rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu dag
9b1(phal chen): bste bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yang dag par sbyangs pa dag nyid che ba ni/ sngon gyi mtha' nas rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing rnam par dag pa'o//
9b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'das pa dang / mabyon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi rgyung du rigs dang ldan par 'byung ba'i bdag nyid che ba ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rnam
9b3(phal chen): bar dag pas rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par shes pa la mi gnas pa ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
9b4(phal chen): bdag nyid che ba ni/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug par gnas pas rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dus gsum la mi
9b5(phal chen): gnas par rnam par spyod cing chos thams cad la rten pa yang dag par bcom pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin/
9b6(phal chen): tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dngos po rnam pa tha dad pa la rnam par gzhag pa gcig gis len pa med pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag
9b7(phal chen): nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mthar chos kyi dbyings la gnas pas
10a1(phal chen): mnyam pa'i bsod nams mi zad pa dang ldan pas mi zad pa'i bsod nams mnga' ba ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba
10a2(phal chen): med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gzugs dang kha dog mtha' yas pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na sems can 'dul ba'i dus dang dbang gis chags pa med
10a3(phal chen): par bzhugs pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par das pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mi 'jigs pa bzhi
10a4(phal chen): brnyes pas bag tsha ba mi mnga' bar bzhugs shing khyu mchog dang seng ge'i nga ro 'byin te/ rgol ba'i nang na stag lta bu'i mthu dang ldan la/ chos thams cad bstan pa la thugs sgron ma lta bu mnga' bas/
10a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas
10a6(phal chen): bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa zhig lon yang / mtshan gyi tshig thos pa tsam gyis bzhugs pa dang 'dra bar sems can rnams kyi yon shin tu sbyong zhing / mya ngan las 'das nas de srid kyi yun ring po
10a7(phal chen): 'das kyang sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i yon zad par mi 'gyur bas/ sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
10b1(phal chen): rnams 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dag na bzhugs shing 'jig rten gyi khams rgyang ring po na bzhugs kyang / 'jig rten gyi khams 'di na gnas pa'i sems can
10b2(phal chen): rnams kyis rjes su dran par byas na sku mngon par ston pa mdzad pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnas kyi bdag mi che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/ kye rgyal
10b3(phal chen): ba'i sras cu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/
10b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rnam pa dag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi tshangs pa'i spyod pa rnam par dag pa la/ sngon gyi smon lam gyis
10b5(phal chen): shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chags pa med pa'i tshul khrims kyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can tham cad kyi
10b6(phal chen): mongs pa sel bas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing gis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'khor gyis shin tu rnam
10b7(phal chen): par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam ni rigs rnam par dag pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam ni gzugs kyi sku'i mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po rnam
11a1(phal chen): par dag pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi sku rnyog pa med pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
11a2(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi phung po bsgribs pa med pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa thams cad la mthu chen po brnyes shing
11a3(phal chen): pha rol tu phyin pa dam pa brnyes pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rnam par dag pa'o//
11a4(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'byung zhing dus thams cad du gnas pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs
11a5(phal chen): rgyas rjes su dran pa'i thob pa'i sems can rnams la dus thams cad du sangs rgyas bstan pa dang / sems can sems cad shes dang ldan pa rnams la dus thams cad du chos bstan pa dang / sems can sangs
11a6(phal chen): rgyas la dad pa'i sems dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dus thams cad du bskyed pa dang / chos kyi skyon med par 'das pa'i sems can rnams dus thams cad du ye shes khongs su chud par bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad/
11a7(phal chen): du sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa dus thams cad du rgyun mi 'chad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du dus thams cad du chags pa mi mnga' bar gshegs pa dang / sems
11b1(phal chen): can thams cad la thugs rje chen po dus thams cad du mi gtong ba dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa dus thams cad du thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom
11b2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs dus thams cad du thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos kyi dbyings gnas pa'i sangs rgyas dus thams cad
11b3(phal chen): du 'byung ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'byung zhing dus thams cad du gnas pa'o//
11b4(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'i tshul rnams te/
11b5(phal chen): bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni nga bzhin gshegs pa'i skus ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ni sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las tshad med
11b6(phal chen): pa brnyes pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi spyan gyi yul mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
11b7(phal chen): rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba tshang med pas bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' bas ye shes rgya tsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi char mngon par 'bebs pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi
12a1(phal chen): zang ba'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang legs pa mang po mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho me med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
12a2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi mtha'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i smon lam dang khyad par mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni phyi ma'i mtha'i mur 'gro ba
12a3(phal chen): thams cad sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las rgyun mi 'chad par sgrub pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi rigs thams cad ma lus pa'i sems dang /
12a4(phal chen): spyod pa la ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams zil gyis mi non pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i
12a5(phal chen): sras bcu po de dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di
12a6(phal chen): ngag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshul rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad kyis mngon par byung ba 'di ni sangs rgyas
12a7(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ chos thams cad la mi mkhyen pa gang yang mi mnga' ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/
12b1(phal chen): grubs che chen po dang ldan pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam min no// 'di / thams cad kyang gongs brgya tshang med pa dang ldan pa'adi ni sang sa sa
12b2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ thams cad snang bla na med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di
12b3(phal chen): lta ste thams cad kyang sems can 'dul ba yang dag par zhugs pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste thams cad kyang 'gro ba thams cad kyi don du/
12b4(phal chen): mngon par sangs rgyas pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ 'dul ba'i sems can rnams 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom
12b5(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ mi gnyis par yang dag par spyod pa'i mtshan nyid kyi chos la rab tu gzhol ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no//
12b6(phal chen): 'di lta ste/ ji ltar yongs su smin par gyur pa dang dul bar gyur pa'i sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi yul mu med pas/ sangs rgyas kyi yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba ston pa 'di na
12b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshul lo// / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag mi
13a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgo rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
13a2(phal chen): 'das rnams ni sems can gyi khams shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi spyod pa sna tshogs shin tu bstan
13a3(phal chen): pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad kyi las dang rnam par smin pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o//
13a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad la gdams ngag dang man ngag shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems/
13a5(phal chen): can mtha' yas pa rnam par sbyong ba'i nan tan gyi sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad la gdams ngagra dang man ngag
13a6(phal chen): gis yongs su gzhog pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i khyad par gyi smon lam rnam pa tha dad pas 'byung ba shin tu bstan pa'i/
13a7(phal chen): sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khyams thams cad ma lus pa'i 'du ba dang 'jig pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o//
13b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa dang mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o//
13b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du 'das pa dang // mabyon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa ni bskal pa yang
13b3(phal chen): bde dang de dag tu bstan cing brjod pa dang / yongs su bshad pas sangs rgyas kyi ye shes thams cad khong du chu bar bya ba'i sgor mtha' yas pa ste// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni
13b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgo'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
13b5(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sems can rnams la sgrub pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku yongs su bstan pa ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin/
13b6(phal chen): las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mdzad
13b7(phal chen): pa'ang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mi mdzad pa'ang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'dzin las sgrub bo//
14a1(phal chen): sa dang / chu dang / me dang / rlung gis kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
14a2(phal chen): 'das rnams ni byin gyi rlabs kyi yul dang mangs dmigs pa thams cad yul du mdzad pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
14a3(phal chen): kyi mtshan kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni zhing la dmigs par mdzad pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin
14a4(phal chen): las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
14a5(phal chen): 'das rnams mi gsung bar bzhugs pa'ang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub ste// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs
14a6(phal chen): rgyas kyi 'phrin las sems can rnams sgrub pa'o// // bam po drug cu rtsa bzhi pa// / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas
14a7(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos te/ bcu gang zhe na/ smon lam chen po la rab tu brtan zhing smon lam zhig pa mi mnga' bas ji skad du gsung ba de ltar mdzad cing gnyis
14b1(phal chen): su mi gsung ba 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos dang po'o// phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thub pa'i bskal pa thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la yon tan thams cad yongs su rdzogs par
14b2(phal chen): mdzad ba rab tu brtson zhing / snying lug pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos gnyis pa'o// sems can 'dul bar 'gyur ba gtsug cig gzigs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du
14b3(phal chen): med pa'i yang brjod du med par gshegs shing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gshegs pa la thags thogs med pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos gsum pa'o// zhe sdang
14b4(phal chen): ba'i sems can rnams la thugs rje chen pos snyoms pa dang / dad pa'i sems can rnams la thugs rje chen pos snyoms pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bzhi pa'o// gang gi
14b5(phal chen): tshe bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas kyi bar du de bzhin gshegs
14b6(phal chen): pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur ro snyam dru byang chub kyi sems mnyam pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos lnga pa'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yang
14b7(phal chen): dag par bsgrub cing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngo bas 'jug gi/ 'jig rten pa'i rgyud lam yin pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos drug pa'o// sangs rgyas thams
15a1(phal chen): cad kyi rjes su bsngo na sangs rgyas kyis spyad pa'i sems su lus kyi las dang / ngag gi las dang / yid kyi las kyis slob cing / nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas/
15a2(phal chen): kyi spyod pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngo ba med pas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bdun pa'o// /
15a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i sems rnam par dag cing 'od gsal la dngas pa thams cad du snang zhing kun tu 'od 'byung ba/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la snang zhing thams cad du snyoms pas
15a4(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yongs su rdzogs par byed pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos brgyad pa'o// 'jig rten pa'i bde ba thams cad yongs su spangs te/ 'jig rten pa'i dga'
15a5(phal chen): ba thams cad la ma chags pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyis gos pa med pa'i smon lam thams cad du mnyam pa nyid kyis 'jig rten thams cad bde ba thams cad dang ldan par byas te/ sdug
15a6(phal chen): bsngal dang spros pa thams cad rab tu 'jom pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos dgu pa'o// sdug bsngal gyi mi bde ba thams cad nyams su bab ste/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi don du dka' thub
15a7(phal chen): kyis shin tu gdungs kyang sla bar sems bskyed pas sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs yongs su bsrung ba dang ldan pa dang stobs bcu'i sa'i bar du sangs rgyas kyi yul la mos pas mthar thug
15b1(phal chen): pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bcu pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos so// kye rgyal ba'i
15b2(phal chen): sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chags pa med pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig
15b3(phal chen): rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du gshegs pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad na bzhugs
15b4(phal chen): pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na bzhugs pa dang / bzhengs pa dang bzhud pas chags pa mi
15b5(phal chen): mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du chos ston pas chag pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin
15b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi dga' ldan gyi gnas na bzhugs kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs
15b7(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar byung ba'i mtha' la chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa
16a1(phal chen): yin sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad tsam gyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor na bzhugs kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod
16a2(phal chen): pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa la gzigs shing thugs kyi skad cig gcig la cho 'phrul chen po gsum gyis sems can rnam
16a3(phal chen): par 'dul yang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gcig gis kyang tshad med bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa/
16a4(phal chen): chen por rnam par spyod kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi khams 'byam klas pa ma lus po thams cad du
16a5(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i chos ma lus pa thams cad kyi mthar thug pa bsam gyis mi khyab par ston cing gsung yang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de
16a6(phal chen): ngag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chags pa med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs
16a7(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku mtshan dang dpe byad bzang /
16b1(phal chen): po sna tshogs kyis rnam par brgyan pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung yan lag
16b2(phal chen): mchog dam pa drug bcu dang ldan zhing yan lag lnga brgyas yongs su bzung ba dang / rgyan brgya stong du mas rab tu brgyan pa dang dbyangs kyi yan lag mtha' yas mu med pas rnam par dag
16b3(phal chen): pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi don dang / tshig dang / yi ge brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pas rab tu tshim par mdzad pa dang / bag tsha ba mi mnga' bas seng ge'i
16b4(phal chen): nga ro chen po sgrogs pa dang / 'jigs pa med pa chen pos bsnyengs pa mi mnga' bar gyur pa dang / chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du sems can thams cad la grag cing bsal te
16b5(phal chen): khong du chung bar 'gyur ba dang / sems can bsam pa tha dad pa dang / dbang po tha rang ba rnam pa sna tshogs 'dul bar nye bar gnas pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
16b6(phal chen): kyi gsung gi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi 'phrin las ni stobs bcus brgyan pa sangs rgyas kyi ti nge 'dzin chen po thams
16b7(phal chen): cad kyi me tog shin tu rgyas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad kyi rgyan gyis shin tu brgyan cing bsgrubs pas chags pa med pa'i spyod yul dang ldan pa chos kyi dbyings kyi
17a1(phal chen): bzhi la rab tu rten pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos gting med pa rab tu brnyes pa/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi rgyan du gyur pa
17a2(phal chen): dus gsum gyi chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can kun gyi sems dang spyod pa thams cad skad cig gcig dang ldan pa'i shes rab kyis rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ 'di ni
17a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'od zer bye ba brjod du med pa rab tu 'gyed par mdzad de
17a4(phal chen): 'od zer de dag re re la'ang 'od zer gyi 'khor gyi dra ba brjod du med pa dang ldan pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus par snang bar byed cing / 'jig rten gyi khams
17a5(phal chen): kyi rgyud thams cad mun pa med par ston pa/ sangs rgyas skye ba dang mi 'bral bas sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las phyir mi ldog cing don yod pa/ sangs rgyas skye ba brjod du med pas gnas pa
17a6(phal chen): med par rang bzhin rnam par dag cing kun tu snyoms par 'byung ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od zer gyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
17a7(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams bzhad mo 'dzum par ston na/ zhal gyi sgo nas 'od zer kha dog sna tshogs kha dog du ma dang ldan pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams
17b1(phal chen): ma lus pa thams cad snang bar byed pa/ sems can gyi khams tshang med grangs med bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnam par ston pa/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu rnam pa gzhan
17b2(phal chen): du mi 'gyur bar lung ston pa/ 'gro ba thams cad du shin tu gsal ba 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bzhang mo 'dzum pa bstan pa'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o//
17b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku ni tshad med pa ste/ bsgribs pa med pas rnam par dag pa chos thams cad chags pa med pa nyid kyi mthar thug pa mtha' dang dbus med
17b4(phal chen): ba'i chos kyi dbyings la gnas pa 'jig rten thams cad dang ma 'dres pa 'jig rten thams cad dang 'dzi ba med pa 'jig rten thams cad kyi de kho na nyid la yang dag par zhugs pa
17b5(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad las gyen du 'phags pa/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyis yang dag par spyod pa/ tshig gi lam dang bral ba/ brjod du med pa'i mthar phyin pa phung po dang /
17b6(phal chen): khams dang / skye mched dang bral ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'od tshad med pa mnga' ba ste/
17b7(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du 'ong ma 'dres shing rgyan du ma dang ldan pa kha dog sna tshogs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa 'od kyi snang ba kun tu thogs pa med cing
18a1(phal chen): thams cad du chags pa med pa/ 'od kyi dkyil 'khor bsgribs pa med pa tshad med pa'i mdzod du gyur pa/ 'od thams cad kyi 'byung gnas su gyur pa ste/ 'a
18a2(phal chen): ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni kha dog mtha' yas pa mnga' ba ste/ kha dog yid du 'ong
18a3(phal chen): ba mnga' ba'o// kha dog 'od gsal ba mnga' ba'o// kha dog tshad med pa mnga' ba'o// sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi bsam pa dang mos pa bzhin du rnam par
18a4(phal chen): dmigs pa'i kha dog mnga' ba'o// de ma yin pa'i kha dog gzhan khams gsum du gtogs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pa'i kha dog mnga' ba'o// kha dog thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin
18a5(phal chen): pa brnyes pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni kha dog bla na med pa mnga' ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi kha dog rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o//
18a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge bas shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/ 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs dge ba rin po che'i
18a7(phal chen): 'byung gnas su gyur pa la shin tu byung ba'o// chos nyid kyi rnam pa thams cad du khyad par yod pa dang / khyad par med pa'i spyod pas rnam par dag pa'i rgyan gyi ye shes skye ba thams cad nang
18b1(phal chen): du gtogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs bsgribs pa med pa'i rgyud rnam par dag pas 'jig rten gyi mi snyan pa thams cad kyis mi snyan pa brjod du med pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom
18b2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang rgyud rnam par dag pa'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byams pa chen po'i mthu dang rang bzhin gyi
18b3(phal chen): rkyen mnga' bste/ shin tu dang ba yongs su rtog pa'i rnyog pa mi mnga' sku'i 'phrin las yongs su bstsal ba/ blta ba mi skyo bzugs shin tu rnam par bsal ba/ thugs rje chen po mngar
18b4(phal chen): ba'agro ba thams cad skyob pa yon gyi gnas kyi dam pa bla na med pa yongs su 'dzin pa'i nang na thugs brtse ba can phan par mdzad pa/ sems can thams cad kyi don du ye shes chen
18b5(phal chen): po byin gyis brlabs te/ bsod nams chen pos yongs su 'phags pa/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing du gyur pa/ sems can rnams kyi yon tan dang ye shes kyi phung po thams
18b6(phal chen): cad rnam par 'phel bar mdzad pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi byams pa chen po dang / thugs rje chen po'i mthar thug pa'i bsod nams kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med
18b7(phal chen): pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni
19a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/
19a2(phal chen): chos thams cad la mnga' ba dang / chos thams cad la snang bar mdzad pa'i mnga' sbyar bas tshig dang yi ge mtha' yas pa la thogs pa mi mnga' ba'i spong pa mnga' ba dang / chos
19a3(phal chen): thams cad ma lus par yongs su brjod pas mnga' che ba ste/ 'dri ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos dang po'o//
19a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can ji ltar yongs su smin pa dang / smon lam ji ltar btab pa'i tshul bzhin du 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mnga' bas mnga' che ba ste/ 'di
19a5(phal chen): ni sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos gnyis pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad sems can gcig la'ang gnod pa med par
19a6(phal chen): rnam pa drug tu rab tu bskyod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rgyan rnam par bkod pa grangs med tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa thams cad gcig nas gcig tu
19a7(phal chen): 'phang ba dang / gcig nas gcig tu gzhug pa dang / gcig nas gcig tu bsdu ba dang / gcig nas gcig tu bsre ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan dang gzhan dag gzhan dang
19b1(phal chen): gzhan gyi phyogs su rab tu bzhag kyang / sems can gyi khams rnams 'khor cing rmongs par mi 'gyur la the tsom du mi 'gyur bar mdzad pas mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen
19b2(phal chen): pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos gsum pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad byin gyis rlob pa'i ye shes kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyan pan
19b3(phal chen): tshun du byin gyis brlab pa dang / thugs skad cig gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rgyan yang dag par bstan pa dang / bskal pa grangs med par brjod kyang yi ge shin tu bstan pa zad mi shes
19b4(phal chen): pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad rgyan thams cad kyis rnam par brgyan pa dang mi mthun pa med cing nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig tu yongs
19b5(phal chen): su 'du bar sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa thams cad byin gyis brlab pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos
19b6(phal chen): bzhi pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i sems can gzigs na sems can gcig gi don du bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par skyil mo krung
19b7(phal chen): gcig gis bzhugs na yang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku la mi bde ba mi mnga' zhing thugs la mi bde ba mi mnga' ste/ gang zag de'ang mi bsnyel bas 'dul ba'i dus las mi 'da' ba dang
20a1(phal chen): gang zag gcig la ji lta ba bzhin du rim pa rim pas 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i sku tshe la mnga' bar byin gyis brnya te bzhugs kyang
20a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la skyob mi mnga' ba ste/ de ltar sems can gyi khams thams cad mthar gyis rim pas sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i gang zag gi don du yongs su skyong ba mdzad pa
20a3(phal chen): la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos lnga pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa/
20a4(phal chen): thams cad du yang dag par gzhol ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i bzhud pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du bzhud pa la thags thogs mi mnga' ba dang / phyogs bcu'i chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa
20a5(phal chen): thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa dang / phyogs kyi dra ba'i rgyud thams cad du thugs skad cig gcig dang ldan pas bzhud par byin gyis rlob cing chos kyi dbyings shin tu
20a6(phal chen): bstan pa khong du chud par byas pas/ chos kyi 'khor lo thogs pa med pa rab tu bskor ba la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos
20a7(phal chen): drug pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'dul ba'i sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi don du thugs skad cig re re la bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par
20b1(phal chen): brkyang rta bar mnga' che ba ste/ del chos thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas pa'ang gang yang med la mngon par sangs rgyas pa'ang med de/ mngon par 'chang rgyu bar 'gyur ba med kyang / spyong
20b2(phal chen): pa'i sa la gnas shing mngon par 'tshang rgya bar yang mi brjod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyang bsgribs pa med par rtogs par thugs su chud pas sems can thams cad 'dul ba'i don
20b3(phal chen): du ye shes tshad med pa'i tshul gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa chen po'i yul yongs su rgyun mi bcod pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga'
20b4(phal chen): chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos bdun pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi spyan gyi skye mched kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las gang bsgrub pa de snyan gyi skye mched kyis yongs su
20b5(phal chen): grub par mdzad do// snyan gyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las gang bsgrub pa de shangs kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do// shangs kyi skye mched kyis
20b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las gang bsgrub pa de ljags kyi skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do// ljags kyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las gang bsgrub pa de
20b7(phal chen): ni sku'i skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do// sku'i skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las gang bsgrub pa de thugs kyi skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do//
21a1(phal chen): thugs kyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las gang bsgrub pa de 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi dmigs pa 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig/
21a2(phal chen): rten las 'das pa sna tshogs rnam par phye ba thams cad du grub par mdzad do// de bzhin du dmigs pa thams cad re re yang sbrel zhing sgrub pas sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las sgrub pa la mnga'
21a3(phal chen): che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos brgyad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rang gi sku'i ba spu'i/
21a4(phal chen): bu ga gcig gi nang du sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad gzud bar mdzad cing khongs su chud par mdzad pa dang / sems can re re zhing brjod du med pa tsam du yangs par mdzad
21a5(phal chen): kyang sems can de dag la gnod pa dang mi bde bar mi 'gyur ba dang / de dag tu 'ang sems can re re zhing 'jig rten gyi khams gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pas bskal pa grang med pa zad par gnas/
21a6(phal chen): bar bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med par gom pa gcig gis phyin pas 'jig rten gyi khams de dag tu sangs rgyas byung ba rnams kyi spyan sngar 'gro bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas
21a7(phal chen): de dag byung ba'i tshe'ang brjod du med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud dang gling nga dag na semasas gyi gtso bo sa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar bya ba dang
21b1(phal chen): ba spu'i bu ga de nas sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa 'byung bar bya ba dang / sems can gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa'i yang
21b2(phal chen): brjod du med pa 'byung bar bya ba dang / chos kyi 'khor lo gcig nas gcig tu brgyang ba brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa bskor bar bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings bstan pa gcig nas
21b3(phal chen): gcig tu brgyud pa'i brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa shin tu bstan par bya ba dang / 'das pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa dang / ma 'ongs pa gcig nas gcig tu
21b4(phal chen): brgyud pa brjod du med pa dang / da ltar byung ba gcig nas gcig tu rgyud pa brjod du med pa yongs su brjod par bya ba dang / nam mkha'i dbyings mtha' dang dbus med par bstan pa kun tu mtshams
21b5(phal chen): med par sems can thams cad 'ong zhing 'gro ba dang / skye ba'i skye mched thams cad du 'dod pa'i longs spyod rgya chen po bgegs med pa thams cad 'byung bar bya ba la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni
21b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos dgu pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du pad+mo'i
21b7(phal chen): rgyan chen pos brgyan pa'i seng ge'i khri pad+mo'i snying po can la de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa thams cad du khyab pa'i skus byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te/
22a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongs su bstan pa mdzad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi ji lta bar 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu tha
22a2(phal chen): bsnyed kyi sems can gyi gtso bo thams cad kyang de bzhin du dgongs pa skad cig ma re re'i byin gyi rlabs kyis brlabs pa dang / dgongs pa skad cig la ji lta ba bzhin du dgongs pa skad cig thams
22a3(phal chen): cad la'ang pad+mo'i rgyud kyis yongs su dag par mngon par 'tshang rgya bar bya ba dang / de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings thams cad ma lus pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa rnam par dag pa rgyan
22a4(phal chen): sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams su dmigs pa rnam pa sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i zhing rnam par dag pa 'byam klas pa brjod du med pa mtshan nyid tha dad pa rnam pa tha dad pa'i rgyud tshad med cing
22a5(phal chen): 'byam klas pa dus kyi rgyud grangs med pa dang ldan pa/ bstan pa ma 'dres pa dang ldan pa/ blo tshad med pa dang mos pa shin tu yangs pa dang ldan pa/ mtshan nyid sna tshogs kyi gnas
22a6(phal chen): med pa/ mtshan nyid bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa/ tshad med pa thams cad dgongs pa skad cig ma las dgongs pa skad cig ma gcig gis thams cad yongs su bstan kyang
22a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ched du sgrub pa mi mdzad pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos bcu pa'o//
22b1(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos so// kye rgyal ba'i sras
22b2(phal chen): bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su rdzogs pa tshang med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams te/ brgya gang zhen/ mtshan re re'ing /
22b3(phal chen): bsod nams brgya pa'i mtshan yongs su dag par 'gyur ba 'di ni yongs su rdzogs pa dang po ste/ des sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o//
22b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs pas
22b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// yon tan thams cad kyi 'byung gnas phun sum tshogs pa'i spyod pa yongs su dag pa rdzogs pas sangs
22b6(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang 'dul ba yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub
22b7(phal chen): tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// sangs rgyas kyi mnga' 'gro ba thams cad kyis zil gyis gnon pa yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'chang
23a1(phal chen): rgyu'o// zhing yongs su dag par bya ba yongs su rdzogs pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o//
23a2(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yongs su rdzogs pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang
23a3(phal chen): gzugs kyi sku bltan don yod par yongs su rdzogs pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams
23a4(phal chen): cad dang mnyam pa nyid yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya ste/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las thams cad yongs su
23a5(phal chen): rdzogs par mdzad nas yongs su mya ngan las 'da'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su
23a6(phal chen): rdzogs pa tshad med bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thabs mkhas pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'dra
23a7(phal chen): rnams ni chos thams cad byin gyis brlabs pa med cing spros pa thams cad med par yang / thugs su chud la dge ba'i sgo nas sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyang shin tu ston
23b1(phal chen): cing brjod de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa dang po'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad
23b2(phal chen): la gzigs pa med cing phan tshun du mkhyen pa med do// ma bcings ma grol ba dang / gzung ba med cing bsags pa med de yongs su rdzogs pa med par yang
23b3(phal chen): thugs su chud la sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mnga' dam pa yang brnyes te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos thams cad la mnga' sgyur ba de yang
23b4(phal chen): yang dag pa de kho na nyid ma nor ba rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur ba dang / chos thams cad bdag gi med cing yongs su 'dzin pa med la de kho na nyid kyi mtha' las
23b5(phal chen): rnam par mi 'dra' yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mnga' chen pos chos kyi dbyings thams cad snang ba la'ang rab tu mkhyen pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
23b6(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa gnyis pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mtshan ma'i mtha' thams cad mi mnga' ste/ mtshan ma thams
23b7(phal chen): cad dang mi 'grogs shing mtshan ma'i mngon par shes pa thams cad dang / ma 'dres la de'i rang bzhin du ngo bo nyid med pa dang / ji ltar ngo bo nyid med pa'i sgra'i
24a1(phal chen): tshul thams cad thugs su chud kyang gzugs kyi mtshan ma'i sku gzugs rnam par dag pa grangs med pa dang / zhing gi mtshan ma dang rnam par
24a2(phal chen): spyod pa'i mtshan ma zad mi shes pa rnam pa sna tshogs yang dag par bstan cing bshad ba'i ye shes kyi phung po mun pa med pa 'gro ba thams cad kyi sgron ma chen por gyur pas mun pa med
24a3(phal chen): pa'i snang ba stor pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa gsum pa'o// chags pa med pa'i mtha' ni sngon gyi mtha' yang /
24a4(phal chen): ma yin/ phyi ma'i mtha' yang ma yin/ da ltar byung ba'ang ma yin te/ chos kyi dbyings su gnas pa ni 'das pa 'am/ ma 'ongs pa'am/ da ltar byung
24a5(phal chen): ba'ang ma yin pas/ de bzhin nyid kyi mtshan nyid kyis 'byung ba med kyang sangs rgyas 'byung ba rnams kyi rigs tshad med pa'i phyir shin tu bstan pa brjod du med pas 'das pa dang /
24a6(phal chen): ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba'ang rab tu brjod cing kun tu gzigs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi yul gyis de bzhin du gzigs pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom
24a7(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bzhi pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i 'dzin las dang / gsung gi 'phrin las dang
24b1(phal chen): thugs kyi 'phrin las kyi mngon par 'du mdzad pa'ang mi mnga' la/ yongs su blang ba mi mnga' bas bzhugs shing rnam par phye ba med pa'i mthar thug pa te/ dor ba meng pa'i
24b2(phal chen): chos kyi gnas kyi pha rol tu phyin la bzang ba'i tshul las rnam par 'das kyang tshul grangs med pa'i mdzod du gyur cing / bgrang ba dang mngon par sgrub pa mtha' yas pa dang
24b3(phal chen): 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa sna tshogs tha dad pa'i grangs kyi tshul thugs su chud pa ye shes bsgribs pa med pas gzigs pa rnams te/ chos kyi dbyings ma
24b4(phal chen): lus pa thams cad kyi sems can 'dul ba rnam par dmigs pa la rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs tshad med mu med par mngon par sgrub pa mdzad pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
24b5(phal chen): rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa lnga pa'o// chos thams cad lta ba med pas tha mi dang pa dang / bye brag med pa dang / 'byung ba med pa dang / mtshan nyid
24b6(phal chen): med pa dang / sna tshogs med pa dang / blang ba med pa dang / dor ba med pa dang / rang bzhin med par rab tu mkhyen kyang chos kyi rgyud shin tu nges pa yang dag par sgrub cing
24b7(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi tshul dang 'gal ba med pa dang / rang bzhin med pa'ang yang dag par gzigs pas thams cad mkhyen pa thams cad gzigs pa mkhyen par bya ba thams cad ma lus par
25a1(phal chen): gzigs pas chos la mnga' sbyar ba thams cad kyang rab tu ston la/ de bzhin nyid kyi rang bzhin las kyang mi nyams pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom
25a2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa drug pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs su chud pa'i rnam pa gcig gis gzhan dang gzhan mkhyen par bya ba/
25a3(phal chen): chos de'i skyon med pa las rnam par ma 'das pa/ gnas pa med pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par dag pa/ mnyam pa nyid kyi chos kyi skyon med pas dus thams cad du gnas par
25a4(phal chen): rab tu mkhyen te/ de la'ang nyi ma gcig gam/ zla ba phyed dam/ lo gcig gam/ lo brgya 'am/ bskal pa 'jig pa dang / 'du bas rjes su bsnyag pa dang /
25a5(phal chen): phyir phyogs pa mi mnga' bar dus tshad med pa dang / nyi ma gcig dang / yud tsam gcig gi dus dang / snga dro nas nyi ma phyed kyi dus dang / phyi dro nas snga dro'i dus dang /
25a6(phal chen): nyi ma gung nas phyi dro'i dus dang / nyi ma bgrangs pa'i dus dang / nyi ma bdun dang / zla ba phyed kyi dus dang / zla ba dang / lo dang / lo brgya'i dus dang / bskal pa
25a7(phal chen): gcig gi dus dang / ma med grangs med pa bsam gyi ma khyab pa'i dus nas/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thub pa'i dus su chos bstan pa dang / chos kyi 'khor lo thogs pa
25b1(phal chen): la da / ra na bar myi sa mapa /
25b2(phal chen): ring mi lan du'adu na pa rlo'i 'gyur te/ 'don sangs rgyas bas ldan 'dus rnams kyi sang sa rgyas kyi bams ma
25b3(phal chen): / seMngs su tsam ldan 'das kyi ma sa pa sas ma dus pa pa pa cho 'dam
25b4(phal chen): ni mi'i rdzogs pa nang med pa mnga' ba'o// ba dang pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mangs med pa mnga' ba'o// zadad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa tshad med pa mnga' ba'o//
25b5(phal chen): thadang pa yang dag par mkhyen pa zad mi shes pa mnga' dra'o// ba dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa thogs pa med pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa
25b6(phal chen): mtha' mas pa mnga' ba'o// bran mong ma yin pa'i thadang pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mthar thug pa med pa mnga' ba'o//
25b7(phal chen): thangang pa yang dag par mkhyen pa de kho na dang ldan pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa tshig gi tshul thams cad rab tu rtogs pa mnga' ba'o// chos thams cad
26a1(phal chen): tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mnga' ba'o// bsam pa dang / mos pa dang / dbang po ji lta ba bzhin du chos kyi tshul dang rnam grangs tshul/
26a2(phal chen): ji ltar rnam par bkod pa bzhim dus mtshams med par ston te/ mdo sde bye ba khrag khrig brjod du med pa'i yang brjod pa med pa rnams mdo sde de dang de la thog ma dang / tha ma dang
26a3(phal chen): dbus kyi tshul gyis yang dag par ston te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa brgyad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
26a4(phal chen): rnams ni ming med kyang / ming dang rigs su byung ba'i chos thams cad tshig dang yi ges shin tu dbyangs pa'i dbyings mngon par sangs rgyas pa ste/ mang 'das pa ma yin pa/
26a5(phal chen): dang ming ma 'ongs pa ma yin pa dang / ming da ltar byung ba ma yin pa dang / ming sems can ma yin pa dang / ming zhing ma yin pa dang / ming chos ma yin pa
26a6(phal chen): dang ming yon tan ma yin pa dang / ming byang chub sems dpa' ma yin pa dang / ming sangs rgyas ma yin pa dang / ming grangs ma yin pa dang / ming grangs
26a7(phal chen): med pa ma yin pa dang / ming skye ba ma yin pa dang / ming 'gag pa ma yin pa dang / ming med pa ma yin pa dang / ming yod pa ma yin pa dang / ming gcig pa ma yin pa/
26b1(phal chen): pa dang / ming tha dad pa ma yin pa dang / ming thams cad ma yin pa dang / chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis brjod du med pa dang / phyogs med pa dang / brda med pa
26b2(phal chen): dang tshig gi lam med pa dang / sgra dang bral ba/ sgra'i rnam pa thams cad mi 'byung ba yongs su bsgrubs pa med pa/ byas pa dang rnam par byas pa med pa/ rnam pa
26b3(phal chen): gcig ma yin pa/ rnam pa mang po ma yin pa'ang thugs su chung la/ brjod pa dang sbyad pa thams cad la'ang pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog brnyes pa dag ste/ rnam par rtog pa'i yul
26b4(phal chen): mi mnga' ba dag go// mngon par 'du mdzad pa med pa la rab tu brtson pa dag go// rtog pa dang / kun tu rtog pa dang / yongs su rto pa 'gag pa dag go// spyod pa
26b5(phal chen): thams cad la mi gnas par spyod pa dgra ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'angs rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa dgu pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
26b6(phal chen): rnams ni chos thams cad kyi gzugs ma skyes pa rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ tshor ba'i spros pa med pa dang / 'du shes kyi grangs med pa dang / 'du byed kun tu rgyu ba med pa dang /
26b7(phal chen): rnam par shes pa nye bar len pa med pa dang / rang bzhin gyis zhi bar rab tu mkhyen te/ chos thams cad skye mched kyi rgyud med pa dang / khams rnams mi dmigs pa dang /
27a1(phal chen): thams cad mi 'jigs pa dang chos thams cad bskyed du med cing rang bzhin gyis nam mkha' lta bu dang / chos thams cad dben pa dang
27a2(phal chen): lus med pa dang / rnam par smin pa med pa dang / spyod pas 'byung ba med pa dang / ma grub pa dang / ma byung ba dang / grangs kyis mi brjod pa dang / yod pa ma
27a3(phal chen): yin pa dang / med pa ma yin pa dang / ma skyes pa dang / ma 'gags pa dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa dang / rnam par byang ba med pa dang / skyon med pa
27a4(phal chen): dang gnas pa med pa dang / yongs su gnas pa med pa dang / yongs su smin par byas pa med pa dang / rnam par btul ba med pa dang sems can med pa
27a5(phal chen): dang sems can med pa ma yin pa dang / srog med pa dang / srog med pa ma yin pa dang / rkyen med pa dang / rkyen med pa ma yin pa dang / rten pa med pa
27a6(phal chen): dang rten pa med pa ma yin par chos thams cad thugs su chud kyang chos kyi dbyings thams cad shin tu bstan pa la pha rol tu phyin pa'i dam pa brnyes pa dag ste/ nges pa
27a7(phal chen): dang ma nges pa dang / log par nges pa'i phung po gsum rnam par dgod pa rnams la stobs bcus thugs su chud pa'i ye shes mi 'jigs pa bzhis rnam par dag pa'i
27b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi yul chen po dang ldan pas seng ge'i sgra sgrog pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bcu pa ste/
27b2(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di ngas
27b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las rgya chen po tshang med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams te/ de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs
27b4(phal chen): ma gtogs par lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten dang / 'das pa dang / ma 'ong ba dang / dwa ltar byung ba'i nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis 'jug par mi nus
27b5(phal chen): ba'o// bcu gang zhe na/ phyobs bcu'i nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas gtug pa'i chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du dga' ldan du
27b6(phal chen): skye ba bstan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mu med pa dag la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad de kha dog tshad med pa gzi brjid tshad med pa snang ba tshang
27b7(phal chen): med pa dbyangs tshad med pa/ dbyangs kyi yan lag rnam par dag pa tshad med pa gsung brjod pas rnam par dmigs pa tshad med pa ting nge 'dzin tshad med pa
28a1(phal chen): shwe rab dang ye shes yul tshad med pa mnga' ba'i rnams lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten la phan 'dogs pa mdzad de// bdud dang bcas pa/ tshang ba dang bcas pa/ dge sbyong dang
28a2(phal chen): bram ze'i skye dgu dang bcas pa lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// byams pa chen po'i spyod yul thogs pa med pa
28a3(phal chen): dang thabs thugs rje chen po'i sgro mthar thug pas sems can la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// bsod nams kyi stobs dang mnga' phun sum tshogs pa dang / dbang po
28a4(phal chen): rnam par sbyang ba dang / cang shes kyi sems yongs su dag pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// theg pa sna tshogs rnam par dag pas kyang sems can
28a5(phal chen): rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// theg pa chen po yongs su rdzogs par bya bas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// 'gro ba thams cad gdon
28a6(phal chen): pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad de// 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las dang po'o// dga' ldan gyi pho brang
28a7(phal chen): nas 'phos pa med kyang yum gyi skur gshegs shing / byang chub sems dpa'i sku tha ma skye bar bstan pa/ sgyu ma lta bur yongs su spyod pa/ sprul pa lta bu'i ting 'dzin gyi mthar
28b1(phal chen): drug pa / mi yor lta bur rnam par dmigs pas/ nam mkha'i yul tshad med par khyab pa/ bzhed pa bzhin du skye'ang chags pa mi mnga' ba sdig rgyu ba lta bur bstan pa
28b2(phal chen): nyon mongs pa med pa'i chos la yang dag par gzhol ba/ gnas med pa'i ye shes la gnas pa/ rang bzhin gyis 'dod chags dang bral bas rnam par dag pa
28b3(phal chen): shin tu rgya che ba'i mdzod kyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// khang pa brtsegs pa rin po che las byas pa'i pho brang chen po rin po che'i rgyun mang po ldan pa na bzhugs pas
28b4(phal chen): kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// rdzu 'phrul gyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// yid la bya ba byin gyi rlabs chen pos sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad
28b5(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa'i mdzod chen po yang dag par bstan pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// ye shes kyi nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen pos kyang sangs rgyas kyi
28b6(phal chen): 'phrin las mdzad do// yum sru steng pa'i spyan bzhugs pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi spyod yul chen po brnyes pas kyang sangs rgyas
28b7(phal chen): kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis 'jig rten byin du brlabs pa mtha' yas pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// ting nge 'dzin chen po grangs
29a1(phal chen): meng ba la rnam par spyod cing snyoms par 'jug pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// ti nge 'dzin las bzhengs pa de dang de dag gis kya
29a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// spyod pa'i thog ma la yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po'i mthar thug pa'i bar du thog ma dang / dbus dang / tha ma'i tshul gyis kyang
29a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// sa 'di la gnyis su med pa thams cad mthar phyin par byas nas tha mar 'jig rten gyi grangs kyis skye ba yongs su ston te/ b+ha bas
29a4(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// gzhon nur gyur pas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// byang chub sems
29a5(phal chen): dpar gyur pas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// mngon par 'byung bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do//
29a6(phal chen): mngon par 'tshang rgya bas kyang 'jig rten thams du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin
29a7(phal chen): las mdzad do// thabs mkhas pa sna tshogs kyis kyang 'jig rten sna tshogs/ 'jig rten tshad med pa/ 'jig rten kun tu mtha' yas pa/ phyogs kyi
29b1(phal chen): dra ba'i rgyud dang rigs thams cad kyi 'jig rten ma lus pa thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// zhing gi rgyud ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi 'dzin
29b2(phal chen): las mdzad do// las kyi rnam par smin pa mA lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// sems can gyi rgyung ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs
29b3(phal chen): rgyas kyi 'phrin lus mdzad do// skye ba dang shi 'pho ba'i rgyud ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// sprul pa chen po'i rgyud dang
29b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang / chos dran po'i sgo'i 'khor los kyang sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi
29b5(phal chen): 'phrin las gnyis pa'o// dpe bar spyod pa'i las rnam par dag cing / gdung rabs thams cad du ye shes kyi tshul rnam par dag par sku tshe'i rgyud kyi tshul dang ldan pa/ sems
29b6(phal chen): can thams cad gdul ba thugs su chud pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad cing btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang na bzhugs pa ston kyang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi
29b7(phal chen): 'dod chags dang bral ba'i tshul gyi gnas la bzhugs pa rnams sgra dang / tshig thams cad dang bral bar brtag pas/ dngos po thams cad dngos po med pa las byung bar khong du
30a1(phal chen): chung par bya ba dang / dngos po thams cad shes pa la gzung bar bya ba dang / tshul khrims thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi mthar thug par yong/
30a2(phal chen): su rdzogs par bya ba dang / snying rje chen pos 'gro ba mu med pa la rnam par blta bar bya ba dang / byams pa chen pos sems can med pa'i yul la rab tu rtog par bya ba dang
30a3(phal chen): dga' ba chen pos 'jig rten brjod du med par khong du chud par bya ba dang / btang snyoms chen pos sems la dbang sgyur ba la gnas par bya ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon/
30a4(phal chen): tan gyis rang yongs su rgyas par byed par bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi lus ma lus par mngon par bsgrub par bya ba dang / thams cad du gnas med pa'i lus yongs su rdzogs
30a5(phal chen): par byed par bya ba dang / 'khor thams cad rnam par dag par nan tan du byed par bya ba dang / chos bstan pa rnam par brjod pa rab tu brjod par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi dngos po la/
30a6(phal chen): smos par bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi nyes pa la rtog par bya ba mdzad cing spyod pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa bas rnam par smin pa yang dag par bstan pa dang / ji ltar bkod pa'i
30a7(phal chen): tshul du sem can gdul ba dang / yongs su ma smin pa'i sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang / yongs su smin pa rnams tshul bzhin du 'dul ba dang / zangs med
30b1(phal chen): pa'i thabs mkhas pa mngon par bsgrub pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las phyir mi ldog pa yongs su bstan pa dang / sgo rna tshogs nas chos kyi spyod pa rab tu brjod pa dang /
30b2(phal chen): sems can rnams kyi bsam pa sna tshogs rnam par sbyang ba dang / thugs rje chen po las byung ba'i chos kyi sprin gyis mngon par spang ba dang / thams cad la slob pa'i byams pa
30b3(phal chen): chen po bskyed pa'i cho 'phrul gsum gyis yongs su brlan pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad mthong ba dang / rnam par dmigs pa'i btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang du bstan pa
30b4(phal chen): yan chad du 'jig rten mtha' dang dbus myed par sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las yongs su bstan pa mdzad cing / ye shes kyi mthu chen po thogs pa med pa dang
30b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi mngon par mkhyen pa bsgribs pa med par bsgrubs pa dang / chos rnam pa gsum gyi thabs mkhas pa dang ldan pa'i 'phrin lus kyi mtha' dang / sku
30b6(phal chen): 'phrin las kyi mtha' shin tu rnam par dag pa dang / gsung gi 'phrin las ye shes nyams pa med pas rnam par dag pa dang / thugs kyi 'phrin las kyi mtha'
30b7(phal chen): cing chags pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i thabs la mkhas pas sems can rnams kyi don mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las gsum
31a1(phal chen): pa'o// dbam po drug cu lnga pa// rnam par rgyal ba chen po mnga' ba rnams ni btsun mo'i 'khor rgyan rnam
31a2(phal chen): par phye ba tshad med pa dang ldan pa yid du 'ong ba spangs te/ mngon par 'byung ba'i spyod pa yongs su bstan pas sems can rnams 'jig rten gyi gnas las bskyod pa dang / 'jig
31a3(phal chen): rten gyi mngon par zhen pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'jig rten du gtogs pa thams cad mi rtag par shes par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi tshul la mngon par zhen pa rnam
31a4(phal chen): par bzlog pa dang / 'jig rten gyi dga' ba la sred pa yongs su bcad pa dang / 'jig rten nyon mongs pa byang zhing nub pa la yang dag par spyod par bya ba dang / sems can gyi
31a5(phal chen): don rjes su dran par bya ba'i phyir mngon par 'byung ba'i don la rab tu gzhol ba dang / khyim pa'i tshul yongs su spang ba bstan pa dang / nyon mongs pa med pa'i chos kyi sbyor ba la
31a6(phal chen): yang dag par gnas par bya ba dang / sngon gyi smon lam yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / yon tan gyi dkyil 'khor tshad med pa yongs su snang bar bya ba dang / ye shes kyi
31a7(phal chen): dkyil 'khor chen po brnyes pas sems can rnams kyi mi shes pa'i sgrib pa rab tu bsal ba dang / bdag nyid bsod nams kyi zhing bla na med par gyur par 'gro ba thams cad la bstan pa
31b1(phal chen): dang dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'i nang du 'dus pa pa gro ba thams cad la yang dag par brjod pa dang / bdag nyid kyis ye shes kyi don
31b2(phal chen): gzigs par bstan pa dang / sems can rnams rnam par dag pa'i sgor brjod pa dang / sems can rnams kha na ma tho ba med pa'i sgor sgrub pa dang / 'jig rten thams
31b3(phal chen): cad du 'byung ba'i sgo rab tu bstan pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rgyal mtshan yang dag par bsgreng ba mdzad cing mngon par 'byung ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom
31b4(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las bzhi pa'o// don gcig ma yin pa mkhyen pa dang ldan pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi mthar thug pa rnams ni
31b5(phal chen): chos thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya bar bya'o zhes byang chub kyi shing drung du byon te/ byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bas kyang bdud kyi dpung thams cad rab tu gzhom pa dang
31b6(phal chen): sku'i byin gyi rlabs kyi mdzod kyis chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du rgyas par dbang ba'i phyir/ byin gyi rlabs zad mi shes pa'i mthar thug pas mtha' rnam par spangs pa/
31b7(phal chen): spyod pa tshad med pa rab tu brnyes pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i yul gyis rnam par rol pa'i ye shes kyi don dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan yang dag par
32a1(phal chen): bsgrub pa yongs su rdzogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du gangan rnam par bsam pas yongs su rgyas pa/ sangs/
32a2(phal chen): rgyas kyi zhing ma lus pa thams cad du byang chub sems dpa' rnam par dmigs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dam pa thob pa rnams kyis zhal du blta ba/ byang chub
32a3(phal chen): sems dpa'i thams cad kyi rnam pa dang / smon lam khyang bar can dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi krol 'khor thams cad gis yang dag par bsam pa'i chos
32a4(phal chen): kyi 'khor mo zab mo rab tu bskong ba sangs rgyas kyi yul chad med pa bsams pas byang chub sems dpa' brjod du med pa'i 'byung ba nas su gyur ba/ byang chub sems das
32a5(phal chen): ba rags spyod pa la yang dag par gsos dang byung chub sems dpa' 'khor byed kyil ma ma par dab pa mang du 'jig rten gyi rnams thams pang bangs
32a6(phal chen): gyis kyi dun pa pa'i yus mnga' ba dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa'i sems can gyis rnam par dmigs pa dge pa'i rtsa ba thams cang ba mi nga pa dang ldan pa 'byung ba'i
