32b1(phal chen): mthar thug pa/ sems can gyi rnam pa thams cad dang / zhing gi rnam pa thams cad dang / chos kyi rnam pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam pa thams ca /
32b2(phal chen): dang yongs su smin par bya ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang / dus kyi rnam pa thams cad dang / 'dul ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i rnam
32b3(phal chen): pa thams cad ma lus par mthar thug pa'i rnams 'gro ba ma lus pa thams cad du mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par 'tshang rgya bas sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad de/
32b4(phal chen): 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las lnga pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba mdzad pa phyir mi
32b5(phal chen): ldog pa'i tshul gyis phyir mi ldog pa'i 'khor lo dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyis khong du chud par 'gyur ba'i tshul gyis tshad med pa'i 'khor lo dang / mi 'jigs pa'i
32b6(phal chen): seng ge'i nga ro chen po'i tshul gyis thams cad ma lus par mngon par sangs rgyas pa'i 'khor lo dang / chos kyi mdzod mun pa med pa'i sgos snang bar byed pa'i tshul gyis chos
32b7(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i mdzod kyi 'khor lo dang / ye shes nam mkha'i dbyings ltar tshad med pa'i tshul gyis chags pa med pa'i 'khor lo dang / chos thams cad kyi dngos
33a1(phal chen): po med pa'i rang bzhin rab tu rtogs par bya ba'i tshul gyis bsgribs pa med pa'i 'khor lo dang / sems can thams cad kyi chos kyi mig rnam par spyong ba'i/
33a2(phal chen): tshul gyis 'jig rten thams cad kyi sgrom ma'i 'khor lo dang 'jig rten thams cad du rgyas par 'gengs pa'i tshul gyis thams cad mkhyen pa'i chos brjod pa'i 'khor lo dang /
33a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad dang mi 'gal ba'i tshul gyis sangs rgyas thams cad 'dab 'dres par gyur pa'i 'khor lo dang / de dag la sogs pa rnam pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong
33a4(phal chen): du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas sem can thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa'i rnam pa la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor te/ de ltar chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas kyang / sangs rgyas
33a5(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las drug pa'o//
33a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni grong dang / grong khyer dang / grong rdal dang / rgyal po'i gnas su gshegs pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las
33a7(phal chen): mdzad de/ mi'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / lha'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / klu'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po'i gnas dang / dri za'i rgyal po'i gnas dang
33b1(phal chen): ma yin gyi rgyal po'i gnas dang / nam mkha'i lding kyi rgyal po'i gnas dang / mi 'am ci'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / ko'aphye chen po'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / swa
33b2(phal chen): po'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / sha za'i rgyal po'i gnas dag tu gshegs kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad de/ 'di lta ste/
33b3(phal chen): grong khyer gyi sgor byon mas g.yo ba dang / 'od zer snang ba dang / long ba rnams mig 'thob pa dang / 'on pa rnams kyis sgra thos par 'gyur ba dang / smyos pa rnams dran pa 'thob
33b4(phal chen): papar 'gyur ba dang / gos med pa rnams gos 'thob par 'gyur ba dang / sdug bsngal ba rnams bde ba 'thob pa dang / rol mo'i cha byad ma dkrol ma brdungs par sgra yid du 'ong bar 'byin
33b5(phal chen): pa dang / rgyan snod na 'dug pa dang / gnas nas ma phog pa dang / ma bskyod ma dkrol bar bskyed cing dkrol ba'i sgra 'byung ba dang / bya sna tshogs mang po'i sgra skad yid du
33b6(phal chen): 'ong ba 'byung ba dang / lta na gtang mi za zhing mi mthun pa med pa'i sku mthong bas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'dzin
33b7(phal chen): las mdzad do// mtshan dang dpe byang bzang po bstan pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do/
34a1(phal chen): yongs su gzigs pa dang / rnam par gzigs pa dang / brkyang ba dang / bskum pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las
34a2(phal chen): mdzad do// gshegs pa dang / slar bzhud pa dang / bzhengs pa dang / 'chag pa dang / 'azhugs pa dang / gzigs pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs
34a3(phal chen): rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// chos bstan pa dang mi gsung bar bzhugs pas kyang / sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// rdzu 'phrul gyi cho 'phrul
34a4(phal chen): dang yongs su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul dang / rjes su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul gyis kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul sems can bsam pa
34a5(phal chen): sna tshogs rgya mtsho dang ldan pa 'jig rten gyi spyod pa thams cad rgyu zhing 'byung ba dang ldan pa dge ba'i rtsa ba chen pos shin tu bstan pa/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa dang ldan pa/
34a6(phal chen): sngon 'grogs 'grogs pa byang chub sems dpa' dang gnas pa'i sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams ni sku
34a7(phal chen): gzugs bltan mi ngoms pa'i 'os bya bar gzhal ba dang / sangs rgyas rnams skye bar dkon mo zhes bya bar ming ches par byed ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mtho 'di de bzhinam na
34b1(phal chen): pa'i gsung thos pa ni bsod nams kyi chos dkar po'i 'byung banas su gyur ba'o zhes sangs rgyas kyi stong pa yid la byeng ba dang / 'jig rten thams cad rnam par dag pa ni/ de bzhi
34b2(phal chen): gshegs pa skye ba yin no zhes bya bar khong du chud par byed pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi yon tan bsngags pa ni mtha' yas pa'o zhes bya bar yang dag par lta ba dang / mabyon pa'i sangs
34b3(phal chen): rgyas 'byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs yang dag par bsgrub pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba dang mos pa'i tshul thams cad kyis srungs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mnyes par byed
34b4(phal chen): pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams ni yon tan mtha' yas pa'o zhes khong du chud par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni sems can thams cad la mngon du gyur par rtog pa
34b5(phal chen): dang de bzhin gshegs pa ni sems can gyi rigs bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gnas su gyur par sems pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni zhing thams cad na snang bar khong du chud pa dang /

34b7(phal chen): byas pa dang phyag 'tshal dang / thal mo sbyar ba byas pa dang / rjes su bstod pa dang / spyan drangs pa dang / mchod pa dang / mngon du mthong ba dang / 'dzum pa byas pa
35a1(phal chen): dang sangs rgyas la dga' ba'i sems kyis mos par byas pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'i sgo nas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnam/

37b1(phal chen): par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas la dmigs pa'i rkyen 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad phyin par dgongs pa mdzad pa dang / sku thams cad bshig ste de bzhin gshegs par/

37b6(phal chen): bzhed pa thugs brtse ba can zhe 'am/ lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi sems can thams cad kyi sbubs su rgyur pa/ mgon du gyur pa/ rten du gyur pa/ bla na med pa bsod/
37b7(phal chen): nams kyi zhing nub par gyur to zhe'am sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'byung bar dka' 'o zhes rnam pa de lta bur smre sngags 'don pa dang / mya ngan byed pa dang
38a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas mthong ba rjes su dran pa'i sems can rnams kyi bsam pa dang / yid la bya ba de dang de dag gi sgor sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las tshad med/

38a3(phal chen): dang sems can rnams dad pas mchod par bya ba'i dbang dung / sems can rnams lhag pa'i bsam pa rnam par sbyong bar bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams
38a4(phal chen): yongs su smin par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams yongs su sbyang bar bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams 'dul ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams
38a5(phal chen): bsod nams kyi tshogs yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod pas dmigs par bya ba'i dbang dang /

38a7(phal chen): can rnams kyi bsam pa dang / mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du sku gdung dang ring bsrel byin gyis rlong ste/ lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri ba dang / lha ma yin dang
38b1(phal chen): nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi'i gnas thams cad du 'dul ba dang / mos pa'i tshul ji lta ba bzhin du sku gdung dang ring bsrel byin gyis rnyog
38b2(phal chen): bo// rang gi spu rnam par phye ste/ sku gdung dang ring bsrel tshad med pa/ zangs med pa/ dpag tu med pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du
38b3(phal chen): med pa byin gyis rlob bo// de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod rten gyis sangs rgyas kyi sku gdung 'jig rten thams cad du rnam par phye ba de'i yul dang / phyogs kyi klu'i gnas pang

38b5(phal chen): sku gdung dang ring bsrel mchod par byed par 'gyur bas/ sku gdung gi ring bsrel dang / dbu dang phyag sen gyi mchod rten dang / sangs rgyas bzhugs
38b6(phal chen): pa'i mchod rten lnga 'gro ba thams cad nges par sangs rgyas dran par 'gyur te/ chos la rab tu rten par 'gyur ro// dge 'dun la dang pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro//
38b7(phal chen): yul dang phyogs kyi gnas de dang de dag rkun mi 'chang bar sangs rgyas mchod pa la brtson pa'i bsam pas sbyin pa yongs su gtong bar 'gyur ro// bsod nams byed par 'gyur ro//
39a1(phal chen): mtho ris de dang de yongs su dag pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// rigs dang rgyud kyi bdag nyid che ba rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// longs spyod chen po/
39a2(phal chen): dang 'khor rnam par dag pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// lha dang mi'i phun sum tshogs pa nyams su myong bar 'gyur ro// log par ltung ba med pa'i lam yongs su rdzogs par
39a3(phal chen): 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas byung ba don yod par rab tu sgrub par 'gyur ro// chos dkar po la gnas pa yongs su rdzogs par byed par 'gyur ro// khams gsum pa
39a4(phal chen): lus 'byung ba'i lam yongs su sbyong bar 'gyur ro// theg pa gang la dang pa'i smon lam gyis nges par 'byung bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa de dang de dag la
39a5(phal chen): drin du gzo ba rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la brten pa dang skyabs btsal ba dang / mgon btsal ba dang / dpung
39a6(phal chen): gnyen btsal ba'i sems bskyed par 'gyur ro// de ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yongs su mya ngan las 'das kyang yon bsam gyis mi khyab pa sbyong ba

39b1(phal chen): mang po rab tu bsags pas bsod nams kyi chogs rab tu rdzogs par 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'dzin las bca ba'o// rgyag
39b2(phal chen): ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las rgya chen po tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams so// de dag ni sangs rgyas
39b3(phal chen): kyi byin gyi rlabs ma gtogs par lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis tshad gzung bar mi nus pa'o// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i nyan thos dang / rang
39b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad kyis 'jug par mi nus pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gnyis su med par
39b5(phal chen): spyod cing dngos po rnam pa gnyis su med pa'i chos kyi dbang phyug gi chos rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni lung bstan/
39b6(phal chen): pa thams cad ston pa la gnyis su med par stong ngo // sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can sangs rgyas kyi rjes su dran pa la brtson pa rnams kyi sems dang /
39b7(phal chen): bsam pa brjod du med pa 'byam klas pa rnams la gnyis su med par spong ngo // sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi ron ma lus par mngon par sangs rgyas pas gnyis su med
40a1(phal chen): pa'i sku rnam par dmigs par mdzad do// 'das pa dang / mnon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la rang bzhin
40a2(phal chen): gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o// 'byung ba dang / 'byung ba'i mtha' gnyis su med pa dang / sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar
40a3(phal chen): byung ba'i mtha' gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o// sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad gnyis su med pas dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad gcig par rab tu

40a5(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyis thugs su chud pa dang 'dul ba mdzad pa'i rnam par dmigs pa gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o// 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad

40b1(phal chen): gnyis su med par spyod cing / dngos po gnyis su med pa'i chos kyi dbang phyug gi chos so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
40b2(phal chen): rnams kyi de bzhinam go shegs pa bzhugs pa/ chos thams cad la rab tu bzhugs pa rnams so// bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings
40b3(phal chen): gnas pa'i ye shes zug su chung pa la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs rje chen po mi nyam pa la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
40b4(phal chen): 'das rnams ni smon lam ji lta ba bzhin du 'byung ba la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'dul ba'i sems can yongs su mi gtong ba la bzhugs pa'o//
40b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dngos po med pa la gnas pa'i chos nyid la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku
40b6(phal chen): skal ba mnyam pa tha mi dad cing don yod pa la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rtag tu mnyam par gzhag pa'i thugs lnga bzhugs pa'o//
40b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad nyams pa med par gzhol ba la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chags pa med pa'i thugs/
41a1(phal chen): kyis rnam par spyod pa la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pas grub pa med pa'i
41a2(phal chen): yang dag pa'i mtha'i mtshan nyid la bzhugs pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa chos
41a3(phal chen): thams cad la bzhugs pa rnams so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams cad ma lus par mngon
41a4(phal chen): par mkhyen pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'das pa bgrangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang
41a5(phal chen): ma 'ongs pa bgrangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / da ltar byung ba bgrangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / tshig gi lam mtha' dag
41a6(phal chen): thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / 'jig rten gyi rgyud mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / sems can gyi bsam pa dang shes pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon
41a7(phal chen): mngon par mkhyen pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba chung ngu dang / 'bring dang / chen po dang / rnam pa sna tshogs rnam par gnas pa'i mtshan nyid kyi dge ba'i rtsa
41b1(phal chen): rnams la bsam pa tshad med pa yongs su mi btang bas sangs rgyas kyi ye shes 'bar bar bya ba dang / yongs su rdzogs par bya ba mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang /

42a2(phal chen): dbang po nyams par mi nus pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi bskal pa'i me'i gdung bas 'tshig par mi nus pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad

42b1(phal chen): bzhung dam/ gzims kyang rung ste/ spyod lam 'gyur ba med do// de bzhin gshegs pa ga na bzhugs pa'i yul de dang / de'i 'khor dag tu 'dra de bzhin gshegs

43a1(phal chen): seng kyi 'jig rten gyi khams sbya ba spu'i khung bu gcig gis gzung ste/ b+h+ra ma'i mtha'i bskul ba'i mur thug par bsnams shing gshegs sam

43b4(phal chen): pa'i 'khor yug chen po'i rdo rje'i ri dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rnam pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa la bsgres pa snyed kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyid kyang de la
43b5(phal chen): bsgres pa de snyed ba spu'i khung bu gcig tu btsud de/ ba spu'i khung bya gcig tu ji lta ba bzhin du sku'i ba spu'i khung bu thams cad du btsud de/ ba spu'i khung bu'ang sems can thams
43b6(phal chen): cad snyed du gyur la/ de dag thams cad bsnams te/ de snyed kyi ba spu'i khung bur tshul de bzhin du bshams te/ thugs bstod pa de lta bus de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi
43b7(phal chen): khams thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs sam/ phyogs kyi dra ba thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs sam// nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs sam/ 'jig rten gyi
44a1(phal chen): khams kyi rgyung bgrangs pa sngon gyi mthar gtogs pa nas bzung ste/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par de bzhin gshegs pas bskal pa thams cad

44b1(phal chen): rkyen gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi ning brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu za ba kong tsam du che ba de lta bur gyur la/ sems can gcig gi lus kyi rang jitsam pa de tsam

44b6(phal chen): 'gyur ro// de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams la 'jug pa dang / nam mkha'i dbyings la 'jug pa dang / phyogs kyi dra ba'i rnam pa la 'jug pa re re dang de lta bu la 'jug pa/
44b7(phal chen): rnamam pa'i khams ma thus pa'i dbyangs kyis phas pa chos kyi dbyings kyi mapa' btugs pa/ kwa'i rje ma'i tshogs kyis ga'al ba'i 'jidzi rten gyi khams la 'jug pams
45a1(phal chen): cang re re zhing yang skra'i rtse mo'i cha shas kyis gzhal te/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyis kun tu khyab pa thams cad ma lus pa'i sgra'i nu mo'i cha shas kyi tshad kyis
45a2(phal chen): nam mkha'i dbyings la 'jug pa thams cad du zhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod lam 'di'i tshul dang skyil mo krung gcig tu bzhugs pa'i spyod pas sngon gyi mtha' dang /
45a3(phal chen): ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa zad par mdzad de/ bskal pa 'da' bar mdzad cing bskal pa la rab tu 'jug ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo
45a4(phal chen): che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bzhi pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gcig la dbye sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du/
45a5(phal chen): med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byin gyis brlabs te / dbu re re la ljags sangs rgyas kyi ning brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byin
45a6(phal chen): gyis brlabs nas/ de dag re re'i kyang dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / sgra skad kyi gsung sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu zla ba med
45a7(phal chen): re brjod de// chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i sems can gyi khams thams cad po bar mdzad cing dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / sgra skad kyi gsung re res kyang mdo sde sangs
45b1(phal chen): rgyas kyi snying brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bshad lA/ mdo sde re re la'ang chos bskrun pa sangs rgya sna kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang ba
45b2(phal chen): du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu gzhol bar mdzad de/ chos bstan pa gcig las kyang chos kyi tshig dang / yi ge sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du
45b3(phal chen): med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed brjod par 'gyur la/ chos bstan pa gcig la ji lta ba de bzhin du chos bstan pa thams cad las kyang de snyed kyi chos kyi tshig dang yi ge brjod
45b4(phal chen): de de ltar brjod pas bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du rab tu bstan la/ bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing
45b5(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed zad par gyur kyang / da dung gzhan yang bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med
45b6(phal chen): pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du brgyud cing rab tu ston pa'i tshul gyi rnam grangs 'dis bskal pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bu rab tu bstan la/
45b7(phal chen): rnam grangs 'di 'dra bas bskal pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyeng zad la/ sems can tha ma thad kyi sem gyi spyod pa snyed kyi bskal pa 'das par gyur te/
46a1(phal chen): phyi ma'i mtho'i mur zug pa'i bskal bzang cing 'das par byas kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa chos thams cad blang ba'i 'khor lo bskor ba dang /
46a2(phal chen): chos thams cad rab tu shes par bstan cing lung bstan pa dang / the tsom thams cad rab tu gcod pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / chos thams cad snang bar byed pa ni
46a3(phal chen): chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad brjod pa'i rgyun dang ldan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / ye shes kyi nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen
46a4(phal chen): po'i rgyan dang ldan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad ma lus pa'i ye shes kyi sgron ma chen pos brgyan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / tha dad
46a5(phal chen): ba yang dag par mkhyen pa dang / mi 'jigs pa chen pos brgyan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba rgyun mi 'chang ngo // sangs rgyas kyi sku gcig gi byin gyi rlabs kyis ji lta ba
46a6(phal chen): de bzhin du chos kyi 'khor lo'i sprin chen po dpe thams cad la dpe med par rab tu 'byung bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi nam mkha'i dbyings
46a7(phal chen): kyi mthas gtugs pa skra'i rtse mo'i cha shas kyis gzhal ba ma lus pa thams cad chags pa med par rnam par dbye bas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa stod
46b1(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa de snyed de snyed du thugs kyi sang cig re re la phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bsal par sprul pa mdzad cing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa'i grwa tham
46b2(phal chen): cad las de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku re re la'ang de snyed de snyed kyi dbu mnga' bar gyur la/ gzhung de bzhin du sku re re la'ang de snyed de snyed kyi ljags mnga' bar gyur te/ ljags
46b3(phal chen): re re las kyang de snyed de snyed kyi dbyings kyi yan lag dang / sgra skad kyi gsung chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i sems can gyi khams thams cad go bar mdzad pa byung la
46b4(phal chen): dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / sgra skad kyi gsung de dag re res kyang de snyed de snyed kyi mdo sde bshad par gyur la/ mdo sde de dag re re la'ang de snyed de snyed kyi chos bstan par rab tu
46b5(phal chen): gzhol ba mdzad de/ chos bstan pa de dag re re las kyang de snyed de snyed kyi chos kyi tshig dang yi ge brjod du med par gyur la/ chos kyi tshig dang yi ge de dag re res kyang chos kyi
46b6(phal chen): dbyings ma lus pa thams cad dbyangs kyis rgyas par bkang ste/ sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams can go bar mdzad kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbyangs la
46b7(phal chen): drung pa mi mnga' ste nyams par mi 'gyur la/ thogs pa mi mnga' zhing dma' bar mi 'gyur te/ de lta bu'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor yang bskal pa phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bar
47a1(phal chen): dar du rgyun 'chad par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal
47a2(phal chen): mtshan gyi chos lta pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs dpal gyi be'us brgyan pa rdo rje chen po ltar shin tu brtan par grub pa mnga' ba dag ste/
47a3(phal chen): de dag byang chub kyi shing drung ngu byon na bdud sdig to can gyis sems can thams cad skyed kyi bdud kyi sde gzugs sna tshogs can shin tu mi sdug pa'adzegs 'jigs ltar 'dug
47a4(phal chen): pa rab tu sdang ba'i gzugs can/ 'jig rten thams cad shin tu 'jigs pa'i gzugs can/ rab tu skyi g.ya' ba skyed pa'i gzugs can/ bdud shin tu mi sdug
47a5(phal chen): pa'i gzugs 'chang ba/ rab mchog por 'jigs pa/ 'jigs pa chen po skyed pa/ 'gro ba thams cad gsod pa/ 'jig rten thams cad phreng bar
47a6(phal chen): byed pa/ de lta bu sha stag gis byang chub kyi shing drung dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug par gang bar gzigs kyang byang
47a7(phal chen): chub kyi shing drung na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la bsnyengs pa mi mnga' 'o// bag tshab mi mnga' 'o// bsu btsag kyang g.yo ba med ngo //
47b1(phal chen): rnags kyi ma shas shin d+ha ma zla 'ga' tsam gyis kyang desar rnam pa pa dang pa'i gzugs pa mtshan mArnam pa dang ba 'dzin pa mi mnga'/ shin du /
47b2(phal chen): ba med do// mi bskul to// 'gyur ba med do// rnam par rtog pa med ngo // shin tu zhi ba'o// bsnyengs pa dang bag tsha ba thams cad dang shin tu thul lo//
47b3(phal chen): sdug pa dang khong khro ba shin tu spangs so// sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa rgyun mi 'chang ngo // byams pa chen po'i stobs dang ldan pa'o// thugs rje chen po'i gnas kyis
47b4(phal chen): dbang po shin tu dben pa'o// bag tsha ba mi mnga' ba'i thugs dang ldan pa'o// thugs shin tu brtan zhing nyams pa mi mnga' ba'o// tshu rol gyi sku gnon la phas zig
47b5(phal chen): gyis mi non pa'i thugs dang ldan pa ste/ bdud thams cad dang / bdud kyi ris su gtogs pa'i lha thams cad dang / bdud kyi sde thams cad shin tu zil gyis gnon to//
47b6(phal chen): shin tu sra 'gong ngo // de ltar zil gyis mnan te snga gong ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa la skyabs tshol lo// de dag la'ang bcom ldan 'das de dag cho 'phrul chen/
47b7(phal chen): po gsum gyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'dul ba mdzad pa nye bar sgrub ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ro// 'di ni sangs
48a1(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos drug pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas
48a2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung thogs pa med pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa de dang de dag thams cad du sems can rnams 'dul ba'i don gyis rnam par dmigs par
48a3(phal chen): kun tu khyab par 'byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung de ni ri rnams la thogs pa med do// ri rab la thogs pa med do// rin po che'i rI la thogs pa med do//
48a4(phal chen): khor yug dang khor yug chen po la thogs pa med do// lha'i khyim la thogs pa med do// klu'i khyim la thogs pa med do// gnod sbyin gyi khyim la thogs pa
48a5(phal chen): med do// dri za'i khyim la thogs pa med do// lha ma yin gyi khyim la thogs pa med do// nam mkha' lding gi khyim la thogs pa med do// mi 'am ci'i
48a6(phal chen): khyim la thogs pa med do// lto 'phye chen po'i khyim la thogs pa med do// mi dang mi ma yin pa'i khyim la thogs pa med do// gal te brgya la 'jig rten gyi khams
48a7(phal chen): thams cad na yod pa'i sgra chen po 'jig rten rnam pa tha dad pa'i sgras 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad gang ste ca co 'dres par gyur kyang / de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung
48b1(phal chen): ni 'dul ba'i sems can rnams kyi rna ba'i rnam par dmigs pa la bsgribs pa med pa yin te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung 'ba' zhig de dag gi rna bu'i rnam par dmigs/
48b2(phal chen): ba la ljang nge lham me lhun ne ste/ go bar mdzad pa'i tshig dang yi ge rnams kyang rlag par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthe bo che chen po
48b3(phal chen): stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bdun pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs ni chags pa mi mnga' ba ste/ bskal pa bye ba
48b4(phal chen): khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par yongs su sbyangs pa'o// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad dang rgyan
48b5(phal chen): gcig tu gyur pa'o// rnyog pa med cing rnam par drang ste shin tu gsal bu'o// bdag gi zhes bya ba mi mnga' ba'o// chos thams cad la mi gnas pa'o// nang nu
48b6(phal chen): gnas pa ma yin pa'o// phyi rol na gnas pa ma yin pa'o// ma skyes pa'o// dmigs pa thams cad kyis dben pa'o// zhi zhing gnas pa med pa'o//
48b7(phal chen): rtsom pa med pa'o// 'du shes snga tshogs thams cad la mi gnas pa'o// dngos pa'i rnam par rdzob pa thams cad 'bags pa'o// rang bzhin gyis 'ong dngas/
49a1(phal chen): gsal ba'o// yongs su dag pa'o// dmigs bya dang yid la b+hA ba thams cad dang ma 'dres pa'o// chos thams cad nyon mongs pa me ba
49a2(phal chen): yul dang ldan pa'o// yang dag pa'i mtha' 'dod chags dang bral bas dag pa'o// chos kyi dbyings shin tu bstan pa'i mthar thug pa'o// chos kyi dbyings kun
49a3(phal chen): nas mi zad pa dang ldan pa'o// 'du shes kyi rnam pa thams cad kyi tshad dang tshad med pa dang bral ba'o// 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi brjod pa thams cad 'gags
49a4(phal chen): pa'o/ tshig gi lam gyis brjod du med pa'i mthar thug pa'i yul lo// mi zad pa dang chags pa med pa'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa'o// ye shes sngon du 'gro
49a5(phal chen): ba'o// stobs bcu'i rgyan du gyur pa'o// chos thams cad kyis rnam par dag pa'o// thabs mkhas pas byung ba'o// chos sna tshogs dang / chos du ma dang /
49a6(phal chen): chos thams cad shin tu bstan pa dang mi 'gal ba'o// dus gsum du tha dad pa med pa'o// chos kyi dbyings thams cad chos gzhi med pa thams cad kyi mnga'i pha rol tu phyin
49a7(phal chen): ba brnyes pa'o// chos thams cad la mnga' ba'i 'byung gnas dang mdzod du gyur pa'o// chos kyi tshul thams cad la dgongs pa khyad par du rmongs pa med pa'o// zhing gi
49b1(phal chen): rlung du gtogs pa thams cad dang / phyogs kyi dra ba dang / rgyud 'bum zas pa ma lus pa thams cad la mi gnas pa brtan zhing mi g.yol nyams pa med pa'i ye shes kyis
49b2(phal chen): rab tu gzigs pa/ chos ma lus pa thams cad kyi mthar thug pa/ zag pa thams cad yongs su zad pa thugs rnam par grol zhing zag pa mi mnga' ba dang / shes
49b3(phal chen): rab rnam par grol bas shin tu rnam par grol ba yang dag pa'i mtha' mi zad pas klas pa chags pa med par rnam par spyod pa/ rtag tu mnyam par gzhag pa/ dus
49b4(phal chen): gsum thams cad ngu bsgribs pa med par 'byung ba/ sems can thams cad kyi dus gsum gyi sems dang spyod pa thams cad ma lus par thugs skad cig gis rab tu mkhyen pa
49b5(phal chen): 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos brgyad pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom
49b6(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku ni sku mo mnga' ba ste/ rang bzhin gcig tu gyur pas sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul tshang med pa'i sku'o// mtha' dang dbus mong par
49b7(phal chen): yongs su grub pa'i sku'o// 'jig rten thams cad kyis zad par mi nus pa'i sra'o// khams gsum pas gos pa med pa'i sku'o// brten pa'i skus rnam par dmings
50a1(phal chen): da'o sgrug pa'i bsam pa dang rjes su dran pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyis sku'i rang bzhin yang dag par ston pa'o// bden pa med pa dang brtan pa/
50a2(phal chen): med pa'i sku mnyam pa nyid kyis yongs su dag pa'o// chos kyi sku bzhud pa dang byon pa med pa'i sku'o// 'dus ma byas pas 'jig pa med pa'i sku'o// mtshan nyid med pas
50a3(phal chen): mtshan nyid gcig pa'i chos kyi sku'i rang bzhin no// yul na mi gnas pa dang phyogs na mi gnas pa'i sku'o// ma lus pa thams cad kyi lus kyi sku'o// sangs rgyas kyi
50a4(phal chen): khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' yas pa'i sku'i rang bzhin no// lus thams cad du yongs su gzhol ba'i sku sna tshogs su rnam par dmigs pa mdzad kyang chos kyi sku'i/
50a5(phal chen): tshul gyi rjes su 'brang ba'o// ye shes kun tu snang ba'i snying po can no// sku yongs kyi mdzod du gyur pa'o// chos kyi dbyings rnam pa tha dad pa med pa shin tu bstan pa'i sku'o//
50a6(phal chen): khams gsum ma lus pa thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pas kun tu khyab pa'i sku'i rang bzhin no// mo g.yo mi dgongs pa'i sgra rnam par dag pa'o// yod pa'ang ma yin med pa'ang
50a7(phal chen): ma yin pa'i tshul ngang tshul ma yin par rab tu brjod pa'i sku'o// sems can gyi mos pa rnam pa sna tshogs 'dul bar 'gyur ba'i sku'o// 'gags pa yang ma yin ma 'gags pa yang
50b1(phal chen): ma yin pas 'dul bston pa su'o// yon tan rin po che thams cad yang dag par byung bas shin tu 'phags pa'i sku'o// chos thams cad sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi de bzhin nyid du yang /
50b2(phal chen): dag par bsgrubs pa'i sku'o// rang bzhin gyis rab tu zhing zhing bsgribs pa med pa'i mthar thug pa sku'o// thogs pa mi mnga' bas chos thams cad thugs su chung pa'i sku'o//
50b3(phal chen): thams cad kyi rjes su song ba'i chos kyi dbyings kyis rnam par dag cing 'jig rten thams cad du shin tu rnam par phye ba'i sgra'o// phyir mi ldog cing bsgribs pa mi mnga' la sangs rgyas
50b4(phal chen): rnam par thar pas ye shes thams cad kyi rjes su 'brang zhing yang dag par gzhol bas thugs su chud pa'i sku ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs
50b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos dgu pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ye shes mnyam pa med pa dang mnyam pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa
50b6(phal chen): thams cad kyis thugs su chud pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyis byung ba'o// mngon par 'grub pa'i spyod pa khyad par du 'phags pa'i smon lam dang /
50b7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pas rnam par dag pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyis yongs su rdzogs par byas pa'o// tha dad pa med pa'o//
51a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyis gzung ba'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya mtsho'i sbyor ba'i tshul thams
51a2(phal chen): cad thugs su chud ba'o// smon lam dang spyod pa chen pos yongs su mi dog pa'o// spyod pa thams cad mi mnyam pa med pas yongs su rdzogs par byas pa'o// spyod pa'i
51a3(phal chen): stobs la thub par dka' ba'i spyod pa thams cad kyis mngon par 'byung ba'o// spyod pa thams cad kyi rnam par dag pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa legs par sbyad
51a4(phal chen): pas rgyung dma' ba med pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi tshad med par spyad pa'o// ting nge 'dzin thams cad kyis spyod yul mtha' yas pa'o// lam thams cad
51a5(phal chen): kyis rab tu brjod pa ma yin pa'o// lam gyi yul med pa'o// lam thams cad la rab tu bzhugs pa'o// ye shes dam pa'i stobs kyi tshul mkhyen pa'o// bag
51a6(phal chen): tsha ba mi mnga' bas chos kyi char 'bebs pa'i 'khor lo dang ldan pa'o// dge ba dris pa dang ma dris pa la rjes su mthun pa'i chos kyi tshul ston pa mkhyen pa'o// mnyam
51a7(phal chen): ba med pa dang mnyam pas shin tu dag pa'o// su dang / thugs dang / gsung gi yang dag par spyod pa rnams la 'dzin las gsum yongs su dag pa dang / sangs rgyas
51b1(phal chen): kyi bsgom pas brnyes pa'o// sangs rgyas kyi rnam par stod pas brnyes pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs thams cad bskyed pa'i don du sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyis mdzad pa/
51b2(phal chen): thams cad rab tu 'byung ba'o// thams cad mkhyen pa'i gnas kyi bstan pa tshad med pa'i gnas rtsu ba med pa dang ldan pa'o// mngon par shes pa'i ye shes thams cad kyis mthar
51b3(phal chen): thug par mi 'gyur ba'o// 'jig rten gyi sems kyis spang ba'i shes pa thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// chos thams cad ma lus par mkhyen cing gzigs pas sems
51b4(phal chen): can thams cad yongs su skyob pa'o// dus gsum yangs pa thams cad kyi tshul shin tu phra ba mtha' dang dbus med pa ma lus par mkhyen pa'o// 'jig rten las 'das
51b5(phal chen): pa'i don mkhyen pa'i phyir zla ba'i ye shes thugs su chud pas 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad rnam par dag pa/ phyir mi ldog pa'i ye shes kyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las
51b6(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i 'jig rten thams cad du sbyor ba'o// sangs rgyas kyi sku bzangs pa thams cad thugs su chung ba'i ye shes kyi yi ge med pa'i chos thugs su chung ba'o//
51b7(phal chen): mge snga tshogs rnam par bye ba dang mi ge thams cad smos shing brjod pa mkhyen pas brjod du med pa thugs su chung ba'o// kun tu bzang po'i ye shes kyis dge pa'i chos spang ba thams
52a1(phal chen): cang rnam par dag pa'o// dam bcas pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can thams cad kyi lus dang skye mched ji lta bar thugs skad cig dang ldan pa'i shes rab kyis
52a2(phal chen): chos thams cad khong du chud bar ston pa mkhyen pa'o// chos thams cad kyi don du chos yongs su btang zhing rim zer bya bas thugs su chud pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams
52a3(phal chen): cang ma lus par yul du gyur pa'o// chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad yul du gyur pa'o// dus gsum thams cad la thugs skad cig gis chags pa med par mkhyen
52a4(phal chen): cing thugs su chung ba'i yul dang ldan pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas 'byung ba ma lus par yul du gyur pa'o// 'jig pa med par 'dul ba thams
52a5(phal chen): cad yul du gyur pa'o// thams cad kyi rjes su song zhing rnam par dag pa'i yul thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas pa'o// sa mtshams med cing thug pa'i mngon par shes
52a6(phal chen): pa rnam par sangs rgyas pa'o// sems can thams cad kyi sems dang / yid dang / rnam par shes pa'i rnam pa dus gsum du brjod pa ma lus pa thams cad thugs skad
52a7(phal chen): cig gis mkhyen cing thugs su chung ba'o// sems can gyi rnam pa thams cad las mtshams ma bcad pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rnam pa thams cad la mu med po'o//
52b1(phal chen): dus gsum kyi rnam pa thams cad la mtha' las pa'o// sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog pa mtha byung ba'i rnam pa rnams cad la tshang med pa'o// shes bya'i rnam pa thams cad/
52b2(phal chen): lhag ma ma lus pa ste/ de dag thams cad lhag ma med par mngon par sangs rgyas pas/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes sangs rgyas kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / rnam par 'phrul
52b3(phal chen): bas byung ba thams cad thugs su chud pa dang / mkhyen pa thams cad rgyun 'chad pa med de/ de la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung
52b4(phal chen): ba'i skus mtha' dang dbus med par spyod pa yin/ chags pa med pa'i thugs kyis spyod pas mtha' dang dbus med par spyod pa yin/ thugs rjes chen po'i sbyor bas
52b5(phal chen): dus thams cad du rtag tu rgyun mi 'tshang bar chos bstan pa la spyod pas mtha' dang dbus med par spyod pa yin te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs
52b6(phal chen): rgyas kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bcu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
52b7(phal chen): rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos rnams te/ 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sems can
53a1(phal chen): thams cad dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab cing dpag tu mi nus pa dag go// kye rgyal ba'i
53a2(phal chen): sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thogs pa mi mnga' ba rnams te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dga' ldan gyi tshe ji srid
53a3(phal chen): par bzhugs nas 'pho ba la thogs pa mi mnga' 'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni zla ba bcus bltam pa bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga' 'o// sangs rgyas bcom
53a4(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni mngon par 'byung bar dgyes pa'i thugs kyis mngon par 'byung ba la thogs pa mi mnga' 'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub kyi shing drung du
53a5(phal chen): bzhugs nas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya bas thogs pa mi mnga' 'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs skad cig gis sangs rgyas kyi chos
53a6(phal chen): thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongs su bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga' 'o//
53a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dus bzhin du 'dul ba rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba la thogs pa mi mnga' 'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge
53b1(phal chen): pa'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa'i tshul bzhin du dus la dab par bshad cing lung bstan pa la bogs pa mi mnga' 'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldaran 'das rnams ni dras la bab pa'i tshul bang du/
53b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad pa la thogs pa mi mnga' 'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa' yongs su grub pa lung bstan pa la thogs pa mi
53b3(phal chen): mnga' 'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni skad cig gcig tu sems can thams cad kyis dri ba yongs su dris pa skad cig gcig gis lung bstan pa la thogs pa mi
53b4(phal chen): mnga' ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thogs pa mi mnga' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni
53b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ma thag tu myur du 'byung ba'i chos rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
53b6(phal chen): ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du ngan song dang bral bar 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du bsod
53b7(phal chen): nams yongs su rdzogs pa 'thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du dge ba'i rtsa ba la yongs su smin par
54a1(phal chen): 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can+da rnams myur du mtho ras su skye ba yongs su dag pa 'thob bya
54a2(phal chen): 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du yid gnyis dang nom nur yang dag par bsal ba 'thob par 'gyur ro//
54a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du byang chub kyi sems bskyed nas phyir mi ldog pa 'thob par 'gyur te/ sems can mos pa yang
54a4(phal chen): pa dang ldan pa sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba las byang chub tu sems ma bskyed pa'i rnams kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems skyed do// sangs rgyas bcom//
54a5(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu skyon med par ma 'das pa dmigs pa'i lta ba can gyi sems can rnams myur du skyon med pa 'da' ba'i rgyu rab tu 'dzin to// sangs rgyas bcom 'das
54a6(phal chen): rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dbang po rnam par dag par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
54a7(phal chen): mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du bsgribs pa thams cad byang ba 'thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du snang ba
54b1(phal chen): 'thob cing mi 'jigs pa rnam pa med pa'i stobs pa rab tu rtsom ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bzhin gshegs pa/
54b2(phal chen): mthong ma thag tu myur du 'byung ba'i chos rnams so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rjes su dran pa rnam par dag pa ste/
54b3(phal chen): bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sngon gyi sbyor bas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs nas bcom ldan
54b4(phal chen): 'das rnams ni spyod pa rnam par dag pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni pha rol tu phyin pa
54b5(phal chen): yongs su rdzogs pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni smon lam chen po yongs su rdzogs
54b6(phal chen): bas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yang dag par bsgrubs pas kyang / byang chub
54b7(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi mthar sangs rgyas kyi tshangs par ldang ba la spyad pas kyang bya
55a1(phal chen): rgyab sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i sgonas kyang / byang chub
55a2(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gzugs kyi sku tshad med mu med pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams
55a3(phal chen): kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi yul gyis rnam par 'phrul pa tshad med mu med pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa'
55a4(phal chen): rnams kyis rjes su dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni stobs bcu dang mi 'jigs pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes su dran
55a5(phal chen): par bya ba yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam kyi rjes su dran pa rnam par dag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po
55a6(phal chen): 'di dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rnam par spyod pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / dus
55a7(phal chen): gsum gyi sems can thams cad kyi sems sna tshogs dang / sems du ma dang / spyod pa dang / g.yo ba'i rgyud thams cad ma lus par thugs gcig gis thugs su
55b1(phal chen): chung ba dang / dus gsum gyi sems can thams cad kyi las dang / las kun nas blangs pa sna tshogs cho mtsho dgu rnam pa tha dad pas mngon par 'gro zhing nye bar sogs pa/
55b2(phal chen): mang nyung dang / rnam par smin pa tha dad pa ma lus par thugs gcig gis thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can gyi rigs sna tshogs dang /
55b3(phal chen): sems can gyi rigs du ma'i sems can ma lus pa thams cad 'dul ba'i dus ji bzhin du yongs su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul dang / rjes su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi
55b4(phal chen): cho 'phrul gyis byin gyi rlabs yang dag par bstan pa ma lus par thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / phyogs dra ba'i rgyud thams cad dang / 'jig rten/
55b5(phal chen): gyi khams kyi rgyud thams cad kyi sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi mtshan ma bzung ste/ sangs rgyas bstan pa dang / skye ba dang / rnam par dbye ba ma lus par thugs/
55b6(phal chen): su chud pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba dang / mos pa ji lta ba dang / 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du rnam pa za dang /
55b7(phal chen): ba tshad med par skad cig tu sangs rgyas bstan pa dang rnam par dmigs par bya ba dang byin gyi rlabs pa ma lus par thugs su chud pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams/
56a1(phal chen): thams cad kyi sems can pha rol gyi bsam pa la sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs yang dag par bstan pa ma lus par thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbying
56a2(phal chen): thams cad kyi sems can rnams 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du nye bar len pa med pa'i sangs rgyas nyid du 'gyur bar gdams ngag dang / rjes su bstan pas de bzhin gshegs pa
56a3(phal chen): 'byung ba bstan pa ma lus par thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can thams cad du 'gro ba dang / de dang der 'gro ba'i lam ma lus par thugs kyi
56a4(phal chen): skad cig gcig gis thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can rnams kyis/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa phyogs thams cad du btang ba'i tshul ma
56a5(phal chen): lus par thugs kyi skad cig gcig gis thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can rnams kyi mos pa dang / sems kyi tshad ji lta ba bzhin du sangs
56a6(phal chen): rgyas kyi sku kha dog mu med pa/ dbyibs mtha' yas pa bstan pa ma lus par thugs kyi skad cig gcig gis thugs su chud pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni
56a7(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rnam par spong ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras
56b1(phal chen): bcu po 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzobs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin tshad meng bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnam/
56b2(phal chen): bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang / chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams
56b3(phal chen): cad kyi sems can rnams la 'di skad cig gcig tu chos ston pa mdzad do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems
56b4(phal chen): can thams cad la mnyam par bzhag kyang / skad cig gis sems can gyi khams sna tshogs rnams pa tha dad pa rnams kyang bdag med pa'i mtha' la gnas par yongs su ston to//
56b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi dus gsum la mnyam par gzhug kyang thugs kyi skad cig gcig gi cha shas la'ang mnyam par bzhag
56b6(phal chen): cing rnam par spyod do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi phyogs 'byam klas pa'i dra ba thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rgyud
56b7(phal chen): rnam pa thams cad la mnyam par bzhab kyang / mo zad pa'i zhing gi mtha' la yang bzhugs shing rnam par spong ngo // sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbying
57a1(phal chen): ma lus pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi su mu med pa la mnyam par bzhag kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi sku sna tshogs rnam/
57a2(phal chen): par dmigs par yang dag par ston pa mdzad do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad sgra dang / gsung dang / thugs kyis
57a3(phal chen): yongs su rgyas par rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang sems can thams cad kyi sems 'byung ba'i mdzod sna tshogs la'ang mos pa dang yid la byed pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par spyod
57a4(phal chen): ngo sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyis chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang 'dod chags dang bral ba'i
57a5(phal chen): mtha'i mur thug pa la bzhugs pa'ang yongs su mi gtong ngo // sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'jig rten thams cad kyi rten pa
57a6(phal chen): la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang / thugs skad cig gcig gis rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba brjod pa'ang rab tu ston to// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi
57a7(phal chen): dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa 'byam klas pa la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang / thugs skad cig gcig gis sems can thams
57b1(phal chen): ma lus pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi su mu med pa la mnyam par bzhas kyang/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi sgra sna tshogs /
57b2(phal chen): par dmigs par yang dag par ston pa mdzad do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad sku dang / gsung dang / thugs kyis
57b3(phal chen): yongs su rgyas par rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang sems can thams cad kyi sems 'byung ba'i mdzod sna tshogs la'ang mos pa dang yod la byed pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par spyod/
57b4(phal chen): ngo sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyis chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang 'dod chags dang bral ba
57b5(phal chen): mtha' mur thug pa la bzhugs pa'ang yongs su mi gtong ngo // sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'jig rten thams cad kyi rten pa
57b6(phal chen): la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang / thugs skad cig gcig gis rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba brjod pa'ang rab tu ston to// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos
57b7(phal chen): dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa 'byam klas pa la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang / thugs skad cig gcig gis sems can thams
58a1(phal chen): pa gcig la zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu za ba gcig la 'das pa dang /
58a2(phal chen): byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu za ba gcig la 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang
58a3(phal chen): da ltar byung ba'i zhing gi byung yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs
58a4(phal chen): pa thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / rnam par 'phrul pa yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar
58a5(phal chen): byung ba'i sems can gyi khams thams cad yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang // ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas
58a6(phal chen): kyi 'phrin las thams cad yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam par thar pa'o//
58a7(phal chen): shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las/ sangs rgyas kyi chos bsam gyis mi khyab pa bstan pa'i le'u ste sum cu dgu pa'o// / bam
58b1(phal chen): drub cu ma bdun pa// / de nas byung chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos mtshan rgya mamathong pa'i don du/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag la smras pa/ kye rtsal bar
58b2(phal chen): sras ngagade bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la mi chen po'i mtshan chos kyi rgyun rin po che sna tshogs sum cu rtsa gnyis mnga' bas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu de ni 'khor kun+da nas ngong
58b3(phal chen): zer gyi dra bas shin tu 'phro ba'i sprin rab tu 'byung zhing rgyas par 'gang ba ste/ de la mi chen po'i mtshan rin po che dang po dbu'i dbu mtshams na rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi rgyal po
58b4(phal chen): las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du snang ba bsde bas/ dpal gyis yongs su rgyas shing yan lag dang / nying lag thams cad nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprin rnam
58b5(phal chen): par bkye ba yongs su 'khyil ba'i glong gi dbyings kyis phyogs thams cad 'od kyis rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi dbu la 'phro ba'i 'od kyi dkyil
58b6(phal chen): 'khor glog gi 'phreng ba lta bur 'byung bas/ phyogs mtshams thams cad ngu de bzhin gshegs pa snying po byang chub tu bzhugs pa ston cing / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi
58b7(phal chen): nam mkha'i sprin kun tu 'dal bas chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i rgyal po sna tshogs mdzod spu g.yas phyogs su 'khyil ba'i dbyibs las
59a1(phal chen): gser gi kha dog bzang por 'od zer 'bar bar 'jig rten gyi khams byung ba'i 'od kyis/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i
59a2(phal chen): dbu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan gsal ba'i 'od kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la rin po che'i 'od kyi glong g.yas phyogs su yongs
59a3(phal chen): su 'khyil pa chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsod nams dang / ye shes kyi sgron ma snang bas 'jig rten gyi
59a4(phal chen): khams rgya mtsho thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi sprin rnam par 'jal ba byang chub sems dpa'i mchog rnams la snang bas/ chos kyi dbyings rgyas par khyab pa'i sprin ces bya ba
59a5(phal chen): mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan gser yid du 'ong ba'i sprin sna tshogs kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba rab tu 'bar bas/ de bzhin
59a6(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od zer rnam par snang bar byas pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bsam gyis mi khyab pa snang bar bstan pa'i 'od kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin
59a7(phal chen): gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che ba chuchu'i 'od zer dang / me tog gi mdog gis chos kyi dbyings thams cad snang bar rnam par 'phrul pa'i srin ma
59b1(phal chen): dun bya na'i rgyal ba mtshan cidang lta bar dadu/ rin po che sna tshags snang ba'i man+dan TI kyi 'od chugs pas/ phyogs thams cad rnam par snang bar byed byas/ sman
59b2(phal chen): rgyas kyi sngon gyi dkara' thub dang / dpal gyi ye shes las rnam pa de lta bur byung ba'i rin po che'i 'od zer rab tu bkye ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i
59b3(phal chen): dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dang / rin po che'i 'od zer g.yas phyogs su 'khyil zhing 'phro bra byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul pa/ rin po che'i cod pan gyi
59b4(phal chen): 'od de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyis rnam par rgyas pa su/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rin po che 'od tshad med par de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi rang
59b5(phal chen): bzhin gyis rnam par 'phrul pa yang dag par ston pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi dbu de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che rnam par 'phrul
59b6(phal chen): pas nor bu rin po che rgya mtsho bkye ba'i 'od dang / 'od zer dri ma med pa rab tu 'phros pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i chos bstan pa rgya mtsho rnam par snang bar
59b7(phal chen): 'das pa dang / mabyon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pas chos kyi dbyings kun tu de bzhin gshegs
60a1(phal chen): pa'i gsung gi sbyin 'byung ba zhes bu bu mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul rin po che'i rgyal po sems kyi hrul po dang / An+da nI la
60a2(phal chen): las 'od bkye ba g.yas phyogs su 'khyil ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad du snang ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'od 'phro ba sgron ma'i skyon
60a3(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yon tan rgya mtsho rab tu sgrog pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du nga ro 'byin cing / sangs rgyas kyi stobs yongs su
60a4(phal chen): dag pa rgya mtsho dang / sangs rgyas rgya mtsho 'byin pa'i sprin shin tu yangs pa'i 'od ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i me tog sna tshogs dang rin
60a5(phal chen): po che'i rgyal po bai DUR+Ya'i 'od zer rin po che thams cad kyi 'od zer kun tu 'byung ba'i dra ba/ mngon par 'phags pa las chos kyi lus dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'
60a6(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dang / phyogs rgya mtshor de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa yang dag par ston cing sangs rgyas kyi stobs chos kyi dbyings la mngon du gyur pa rab tu ston
60a7(phal chen): par bzhugs pa/ sems can thams cad la yongs su ston pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa tshad med mu med par yang dag par 'phags shing yongs su dag la dri ma med po
60b1(phal chen): yongs su mnan te/ rin po che thams cad kyi 'od kun tu snang ba'i rang bzhin rab tu bkye ba'i 'od zer dkyil 'khor gyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin
60b2(phal chen): gshegs pa'i mtshan 'jig rten gyi khams tshad med pa na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi mtshan rin po che las 'od rab tu bkye bas/ zhing thams cad klan
60b3(phal chen): nas yog cing bsgribs pa med de/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi gsung rin po che'i me tog shin tu rgyas pa'i 'od zer 'phro ba rab tu bkye bas chos
60b4(phal chen): rgya mtsho chen po rab tu sbyar ba las byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyi snying po dang / snang ba can gyi sprin langs pa'i 'od ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin
60b5(phal chen): gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che bai DUR+Ya dang / in dra nI la dang / rdo rje mang po las nor bu ri no che rnam par bton te/ rab tu bkram pa'i kha dog mtha' yas pa'i 'od
60b6(phal chen): rnam par dag pa/ rin po che bai DUR+Ya'i 'od kun tu 'byung ba las sgra skad rgya mtsho thams cad kyis chos kyi dbyings su sangs rgyas kyi snang ba rnam par ston pa'i chos rgya mtsho'i ye
60b7(phal chen): shes sangs rgyas sprul pa'i 'od kun tu 'gyed pa'i sngon rab tu snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i 'od g.yas
61a1(phal chen): phyogs su 'phro ba'i me tog rin po che'i lbab lhub kyis brgyan pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po byang
61a2(phal chen): nub kyi sprin mngon par 'thon pa/ chos kyi dbyings dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du chos rnam par dag ste/ bskul pa thams cad du rnam par thar pas
61a3(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings rnam par sangs rgyas pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che sems kyi rgyal po'i 'od zer dam
61a4(phal chen): pa rgya mtshos brgyan pa'i chos kyi rgyan du mtshan rnam par bkod pa las 'jig rten gyi khams na 'khod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sprinu lnga snang ba shin tu 'byung zhing ye shes kyi sku
61a5(phal chen): dang chos kyi skus de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mtshan rgya mtsho la spong pa'i byang chub sems dpas yongs su khyab pa'o sprin dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi
61a6(phal chen): ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu lnga de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rdo rje'i gzhi me tog dang ldan pa'i bai DUR+Ya kun tu snang bas/ chos kyi dbyings
61a7(phal chen): thams cad kyi rgyan du gyur te/ rnam par snang bas chos kyi dbyings rgya mtsho yongs su rgyas par 'gengs shing / 'jig rten gyi khams su rin po che thams cad kyi bcwa
61b1(phal chen): 'od kyi rgyan thams cad kyis chos kyi dbyings thams cad du khebs par byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bzhis rnam par 'phrul pa dang / dA ros chos kyi dbyings thams rang dud+has
61b2(phal chen): pa'i mtshan rgyu mtshos thams cad du brgyan pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan chos kyi dbyings rgya mtsho'i gni
61b3(phal chen): gang chen mtsho thams cad kyi rgyun dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rgyan tshad med pa thugs skad cig gis yang dag par bar ston cing / chos kyi dbyings dang / 'jig rten gyi khams
61b4(phal chen): thams cad du bsam gyis mi khyab par 'gengs pas/ sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin rgya mtsho'i spyod pa rnam par gzigs pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs
61b5(phal chen): pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan pad+mo'i gzhi dang / rgyan gyis me tog ri rab rgya mtsho'i 'od zer rin po che'i gzhi sangs rgyas kyi dgongs pa las byung ba dang / rnam par snang
61b6(phal chen): mdzad kyi sprul pa rgya mtsho mi zad pa'i 'od kun tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mda' bA dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dpalnga rin po che dri ma med par
61b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi 'ong sna tshogs de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi seng ge'i khri dang / rgyan dang / sangs rgyas kyi sku'i gzugs pa na mthong na bsrel cing rin po che'i 'od 'gro ba'i/
62a1(phal chen): gni rgya mtsho dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos khyu mchog gi mthu phung ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi tshul gyis zhing rgya mtsho thams cad snang ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa
62a2(phal chen): thams cad kyi rnam par grol ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan bai DUR+Ya'i rin po che'i me tog dang / gser gyi pad+mo las chos
62a3(phal chen): kyi 'od zer gyi sprin dang / rin po che'i rgyal po sgron ma ltar de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od rnam par dag pas snang ba'i rgyun bstan pas/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du dmig
62a4(phal chen): shing rnam par bkye bas tha mi dad cing sangs rgyas kyi dbu'i rin po che'i sprin dang / rdo rje 'od 'phro ba'i ri 'od zer stug po'i sprin gyis chos kyi dbyings la 'jug cing / chos rgya mtsho'i tshul
62a5(phal chen): gyis rnam par 'phrul pas snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan 'khor lo rtsibs stong pa rin po che'i 'od zer sna tshogs
62a6(phal chen): tshad med pa dang ldan pa thams cad du rnam par dag la dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyis phyogs bcu thams cad du shes rab kyi nyi ma shin tu gsal ba dang / ye shes kyi 'od kyi chos rgya mtsho'i
62a7(phal chen): dbyangs dang ldan pa sangs rgyas kyi gdung rnam par dag pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i 'phreng ba rnam par brtse
62b1(phal chen): ba dang / rin po che'i me tog dang / rin po che bai nuR+Ya'i 'od du 'phro ba'i sangs rgyas kyi 'od seng ge rnam par snang ba'i mthu dang ldan pas/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du rnam par/
62b2(phal chen): gnon pa'i mtshan rgya mtsho'i sprin gyi rdul gcig las sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul snyed du yang dag par 'gro bas sangs rgyas kyi mtshan yang dag par ston cing de'i dkyil 'khor
62b3(phal chen): gyi ye shes ston pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mtshan dang / rnam par 'phrul pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi dbul de bzhin gshegs
62b4(phal chen): pa'i mtshan de kho na thugs su chud pa'i mtshan nyid rin po che'i rgyan rnam par dag pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi snying po ched med pa dang
62b5(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings thams cad du snang ba'i 'od la 'jug pa zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che bai DUR+Ya'i me tog dang / seng ge
62b6(phal chen): zla ba 'od zer rnam par snang ba dang / rin po che'i rgyal po 'od zer brgya pa kun tu snyoms par dpal gyi sprin gyis chos kyi dbyings dang / nam mkha' khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi 'od zer snang bas/
62b7(phal chen): ning dang 'jig rten mang por de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa'i 'od rnam par snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan sangs
63a1(phal chen): rgyas kyi snang ba rin po che thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba'i sgron ma chos kyi dbyings kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud kyis kun tu rnam par dag pas sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyi sprin byogs
63a2(phal chen): bcur bkye ba kun tu sdang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i 'od 'phro ba'i na bun gyis byang chub sems dpa'
63a3(phal chen): thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po byang chub tu bzhugs te/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad thugs kyi skad cig re re la byang chub sems dpa'i dge 'dun yang dag par ston cing rgyan
63a4(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa thams cad yongs su ston pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che rgya
63a5(phal chen): mtsho dang / spos yid du 'ong ba sna tshogs kyi 'od zer rin po che'i dra ba rab tu 'phel bas sems can gyi khams kyi las rgya mtsho thams cad sgrog pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad
63a6(phal chen): sgrog pa'i dbyangs kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan yongs su dag pas/ zhing thams
63a7(phal chen): cad kyi rgyan rab tu snang ba rnam par bkod pa'i phyir chos rgya mtsho'i sgra bsam gyis mi khyab pa sangs rgyas nas 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i chos kyi rang bzhin gyi
63b1(phal chen): gzhi sna tshe gas kun tu snang bas/ sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa mang po kun tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan sangs
63b2(phal chen): rgyas rgya mtsho'i sman chos kyi dbyings thams cad du bsgribs pa mi mnga' ba phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du bzhugs pa'i 'od rab tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba
63b3(phal chen): dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan byang chub sems dpa' dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / sems can rgya mtsho bsam gyis mi khyab
63b4(phal chen): pa'i chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa'i tshul mang po chos kyi dbyings thams cad du snang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi sprin kun tu mched pa dang / rin po che'i sprin gyi sgron ma'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba
63b5(phal chen): dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan ye shes kun tu yangs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dang
63b6(phal chen): chos rgya mtsho lam tshang med pa dang / zhing gi dkyil 'khor dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sngo ba sems can gyi rgyud thams cad kyi bsam pa ji bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi spyod yul gyis/
63b7(phal chen): zhugs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang / spyod pa'i nga ros sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyi gzhi kun gyi mthar thug cing thams cad mngon par
64a1(phal chen): mkhyen pas chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi kun tu thug par 'byung ba'i skyon ces bya ba mnga' ba dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs/
64a2(phal chen): papa'i mtshan chos kyi dbyings dang / nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad ngu rin po che snang ba'i smon yid du 'ong ba snying po byang chub kyi gzugs brnyan yongs su ston par mngon par
64a3(phal chen): 'phags pas byang chub sems dpa' dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku'i yang dag par ston pa'i sprin kun tu bkye bas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du smin
64a4(phal chen): gyi 'od du gnas pa zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan gtsug tor 'od kun tu snang ba tshad med pa ston pas byang chub sems dpa'
64a5(phal chen): dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od rnam par dag pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par gnon pa dang / gzi chen pos chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi kun tu snang bar rin po che
64a6(phal chen): rgyal po ltar 'od kun nas 'byung ba yongs su grub ste/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du 'od zer gyi sprin dang / 'od kyi rgyan phyogs thams cad snang bas rnam par snang bar byung
64a7(phal chen): zhing byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs shin tu 'phel ba'i mthu dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par gnon pa'i sprin gyis phyogs bcu'i
64b1(phal chen): zhing gi dra ba dang / nam mkha'i khams thams cad rgyas par khyab pa'i byang chub kyi sems rin po che'i 'od zer gyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu
64b2(phal chen): la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan gtsug tor dbu'i gtsug nas mtho ba rim gyis mngon par 'phags shing 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser dang rin po che'i tshon gyis kha dog
64b3(phal chen): bzang po rnam pa sna tshogs kyi 'od dang ldan par gyur pa/ gser gyi thig le dri ma med pa'i mig 'phrul gyis kun nas shin tu brgyan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na bzhug
64b4(phal chen): pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad thugs kyi skad cig re re la yongs su ston pa'i sprin gyis kun tu khyab par khyab cing zhing gi dkyil 'khor snang bar gyur pas zhing gi dkyil
64b5(phal chen): 'khor byang chub sems dpa'i gnas su gyur pa/ rgyan thams cad kyis rab tu brgyan pa kun tu snang ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i gtsug tor mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis kyi rgyan du gyur cing
64b6(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi rgyun du gyur pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzod sbru la de bzhin gshegs pa'i
64b7(phal chen): mtsham sangs rgyas rgya mtsho thams cad kyi 'ong rab tu snang ba rin po che thams cad du mdog sngar snang ba nyi ma dang zla ba ltar snga ba zhing shin tu rnam par dag pas phyogs
65a1(phal chen): bcur 'od zer rgya mtsho rab tu 'byed pa kun nas rin po che'i 'od zer 'byung ba / 'od kun tu snang ba dpal kun tu rgyas pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sku
65a2(phal chen): rab tu 'bar ba'i sgron ma dri ma med pa'i me tog shin tu rgyas shing rin po che'i sprin chen po shin tu 'gyed pa phyogs kyi 'khor thams cad du rnam par snang zhing de bzhin
65a3(phal chen): gshegs pa'i chos rgya mtsho thams cad kyi dbyangs kyi sgra/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du shin tu 'phags pa'i mar me rab tu snang bas/ rin po che'i rgyal po'i me tog kun tu
65a4(phal chen): nus shing chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'a'o// de bzhin ga shegs pa'i spyan la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshanamatshan rin po che sna tshogs sems can
65a5(phal chen): gyi khams su chags pa med pa'i ye shes kyi spyan rnam par dag pas grub pa/ 'od 'gro ba'i sbyin rin po che dngul gyi mdog tu kun tu ston pas rnam par 'phrul pa'i sbyin ces bya ba mnga'a'o//
65a6(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i shang la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che sna tshogs kyis yongs su dag pas/ rin po che thams cad kyi 'od dang / mdog dang / ma dog dang
65a7(phal chen): ldan par gyur pa de bzhin du thugs su chung ba rin po che'i matog gi sngon thos kun tu rgyas shing / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos rgya mtsho bsamakyis
65b1(phal chen): mi khyab pa dang / sems can gyi 'jig rten thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga'a'o// sangs rgyas kyi ljags yangs pA la 'jig rten gyi kham rgyu mtsha
65b2(phal chen): thams cad ljags yangs pa'i sprin gyis kun tu khyab pa'i mtshan nyid yongs su rdzog pa'i dge ba'i rtsa bas yongasu grub pa/ rin po che thams cad kyi rgyal po'i gzhi las 'od 'phros pas
65b3(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings thams cad rnam par snang bar mdzad pa'i ngang tshul can 'dis pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sems kyi gzugs brnyan dang / de bzhin
65b4(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi dbyings kyi rgyan thams cad shin tu ston pa'i gsung dang ldan pa'i sangs rgyas kyi mtshan gyi ljags yengs pa'i sgo rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog dang mdog
65b5(phal chen): gis rab tu brgyan pa 'od zer rgya mtsho bsam gyis mi khyab pa rab tu snang ba bzhad mo 'dzum pas phyogs bcur rab tu bkye zhing 'gro ba thams cad shin tu dang ste/ rin po
65b6(phal chen): che'i 'od 'phro bas rab tu brgyan par de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung sna tshogs rnam par dag pa rab tu brjod cing / shin tu rgya che ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du chos kyi
65b7(phal chen): ngaro 'byin pa bskal pa tshad med par sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi sgra 'byin pa/ chos kyi dbyings gnas pa thams cad du nga ro yangs pa 'byin pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du/
66a1(phal chen): dbyangs shin tu sgrog cing / snang ba yang dag par ston pa'i dbyangs kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga'a'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i ljags kyi 'og gi drung na de/
66a2(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che sna tshogs thams cad ltar snang zhing mdzod spu yongs su 'khyil ba'i dbyibs lta bu// rin po che thams cad kyi rang bzhin lta bu
66a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsung gi dkyil 'khor phyogs kun nas btang ba'i dbyangs dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi sbubs can ljags kyi mtshan nyid yongs su dag pa
66a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul gyi mtshan nyid med pa'i rang bzhin du sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsung rgya mtsho bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dbyangs sgrog pa'i sprin ces bya/
66a5(phal chen): ba mnga' 'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i ljags kyi rtse mo la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che gser gyi 'od 'phro bas sangs rgyas rgya mtsho'i dbyings thams cad du snang
66a6(phal chen): zhing yid du 'ong ba'i rin po che'i rgyal po'i dbyangs kyi yan lag 'jig rten gyi khams cad ngu sgrog cing gsung snyan pa'i ro myong bas/ sems can go bar mdzad cing bskal pa bsam
66a7(phal chen): gyigyimi khyab par mnyan du yod par dbyangs kyi yan lag gi sgra yang dag par ston pa'i sprin sems can thams cad la yid du 'ong ba'i chos su snang bas chos kyi dbyings rnam par
66b1(phal chen): snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' 'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i ljags kyi rtse mo la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan zhing tshad med pa yongs su dag pa na bzhugs pa'i gsung
66b2(phal chen): rin po che'i rgyal pos kun nas brgyan cing sna tshogs su gyur pas sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi dbyings kyi glong du bsngags pa rab tu 'jug pa rnam par phye ba gzhan dang gzhan
66b3(phal chen): du byang chub sems dpa' rnams la yang dag par ston pa'i sprin gyis chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi dang / sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kun nas
66b4(phal chen): yog par sangs rgyas kyi gsung la byang chub sems dpa' 'dzud cing / zhing thams cad du rin po che'i rgyal po sgro kun nas ston pas chos kyi dbyings su snang ba'i sprin ces bya
66b5(phal chen): ba mnga' 'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhal gyi dkan la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan oMn+d+ra nI la sna tshogs baiDUR+Ya'i dbyibs kyis chos kyi dbyings kyi khongs su gtogs
66b6(phal chen): pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sprin yongs su rgyas par mdzad pa/ phyogs thams cad du rin po che'i 'od 'phro zhing dri ma med pa byung bas/ rnam par snang ba'i spos kyi sgron
66b7(phal chen): ma'i sprin gyi khongs su byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs 'dus par snang bas zhing rgya mtsho'i ming du bya ba thams cad du rnam par 'phrul pa'i tshul rab tu gnas shing chos kyi dbyung /
67a1(phal chen): bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i chos nyid yang dag par ston pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' 'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i choms mche ba g.yas kyi 'og ma la de/
67a2(phal chen): gshegs pa'i mtshan 'od rin po che'i mtshan gyi rgyan gyis chos kyi dbyings yangs pa/ 'od zer snang ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo sna tshogs kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems ma
67a3(phal chen): pa rin po che rnam pa thams cad du mdzes par byung ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku'i 'od gsal bas 'od kyi dra ba kun tu bkye ba/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho'i
67a4(phal chen): sems can du gtogs pa thams cad la bkra shrIs dang / 'khor lo rnam pa kun tu mdzes pas rnam par snang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi tshems mche ba de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprin ces bya
67a5(phal chen): ba mnga' 'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems mche ba g.yas pa gong ma la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rdo rje spos kyi 'od 'phro ba'i sprin kun tu snang ba'i 'od zer rin po che'i rgyal/
67a6(phal chen): po rnam par snang ba'i snying po can chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi tshad kyis glo ba rin po che'i 'od zer sna tshogs rab tu bkye ba'i 'od zer re re'i khongs su phyogs bcu'i sangs
67a7(phal chen): rgyas thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa chung bar ston pa/ zhing thams cad kyi snying po byang chub kyi rgyan gyi kun tu nar cing mched pas 'od kyi sprin rin po che'i 'ong du 'gro ba ri rab
67b1(phal chen): ci nying rnam zhes bya ba mnga'a'o// de bzhi gshegs pa'i choms mche ba g.yon pa 'ob ma lta de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan pa dang pa'i mtshan nyid shin tu ston pas/ rngon
67b2(phal chen): dang rin po che yid du 'ong ba'i me tog sna tshogs thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul sna tshogs kyi 'khor lo dang / rin po che thams cad kyis 'od zer rnam par snang ba kun tu
67b3(phal chen): 'phro ba'i sgron ma dri ma med pa'i sprin yang dag par bstan pas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du rab tu gsal bas rnam par snang zhing de bzhin gshegs pa gangan
67b4(phal chen): seng ge'i khri pad+mo'i snying po can dri ma med pa la bzhugs pa'i sprin byang chub sems dpa'i rgya mtsho'i dbyings su rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi ri rab kyi mar me rab
67b5(phal chen): tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' 'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems mche ba g.yon pa gong ma la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che gser gyi 'od sna tshogs kun nas
67b6(phal chen): rnam par dag pa 'dzam du chu klung gi rin po che'i rgyud kyi dra ba'i 'khor lo dang / rin po che'i me tog shin tu snang ba'i 'khor lo sna tshogs yongs su 'khyil ba chos kyi dbyings su
67b7(phal chen): gsung sgrog cing sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa yongs su ston pas/ byang chub sems dpa' yongs su smin par mdzad cing nam mkha'i
68a1(phal chen): dbyings su rgyun thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan gyi sngon zad mi shes bya kun tu mched par 'gyed pas chos rgya ma rab tu sgrog pa'i sangs
68a2(phal chen): rgyas kyi gsung dang rin po che thams cad kyi tshon du snang ba'i sangs rgyas nam mkha'i dbyings la gsung gi sgra 'byin pa chos kyi sgron ma'i 'di de bzhin gshegs/
68a3(phal chen): pa'i sprin du snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' 'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems kyi mtshams na de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan tshems kyi mtshams thams cad mtshan gcig par me
68a4(phal chen): tog gi mtshan dang / rgya mtsho'i sgo'i mtshan gyi sprin rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog tu 'dal ba las rin po che'i 'od zer rgya mtsho rab tu 'gyed cing bzhang mo 'dzum pas
68a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi 'od nor bu rin po che'i 'od 'phro ba g.yas phyogs su 'khyil zhing / chos kyi dbyings rgyas par khyab par rin po che'i 'od zer rgya mtsho khongs su chud pa'i snying po can
68a6(phal chen): gyis sangs rgyas kyi tshems kyi mtshams thams cad rgyas par gang bas skad cig tu 'od kyis rgyas par kun tu rgyu ba'i 'od zer sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi dkyil 'khor rgya
68a7(phal chen): kun tu 'gyed pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' 'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i spos la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser dang
68b1(phal chen): mdog dang 'od ltar snang ba chos kyi dbyings thams cad du mdungs rab tu snang bas dpal phun sum tshogs pa rin po che thams cad kyi 'od zer dang mdangs kyis
68b2(phal chen): kun tu khyab par rnam par snang zhing / gser dang pad+mo'i mdog yongs su dag pas kun tu sbyangs pas rin po che thams cad kyi mdungs dang mdog tu snang ba mnga' 'o//
68b3(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i mgur la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dung gi mgur/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'od lam me lam mer yongs su snang bas mdog shin tu gsal/
